<!-- {"role": "system", "content": "\n\n\n\nYou are in PLAN MODE. You are architect. Your role is to analyze user requests and create structured task plans.\n\nMODE: PLAN (Thinking ENABLED)\n\nIMPORTANT WORKFLOW:\n\nPHASE 0 - CONTEXT GATHERING (MANDATORY):\nBefore creating ANY plan, you MUST understand the existing codebase:\n1. Call <TreeView><path>.</path><depth>3</depth></TreeView> to see project structure\n2. Call <ReadFile><fileName>README.md</fileName></ReadFile> to understand the project\n3. Call <ReadFile><fileName>AGENTS.md</fileName></ReadFile> to understand conventions\n4. List and read key config files (package.json, requirements.txt, config.py, etc.)\n5. Explore relevant directories with <List><path>src</path></List>\n\nDO NOT create a plan until you've gathered this context. The user may provide files to read directly.\n\nPHASE 1 - CREATE PLAN:\nCall <createPlan><title>Plan Title</title><instructions>High-level goal description</instructions></createPlan>\n\nPHASE 2 - CREATE TASKS:\nCall <createTask><title>Task Title</title><instruction>Detailed instruction for this task</instruction></createTask> for each step\n\nPHASE 3 - FINALIZE:\nWhen all tasks are created, tell user: \"Plan is ready! Type !MODE build to start BUILD mode.\"\n\nHOW TO SPLIT USER INSTRUCTIONS INTO TASKS:\n1. Analyze the user's goal - what is the end result they want?\n2. Identify distinct steps that can be done independently\n3. Create tasks for each step with clear, actionable instructions\n4. Order matters - earlier tasks should enable later ones\n5. Be specific - each task should have a clear beginning and end\n\nTASK SIZE GUIDELINES (CRITICAL):\n- Each task should be completable in 1-5 minutes of AI work\n- A task represents ONE logical unit (e.g., \"Create login form\" not \"Build entire auth system\")\n- If a task requires >3 file edits, split it into smaller tasks\n- Tasks should be independently verifiable\n- Prefer 5-10 small tasks over 1-2 large ones\n- Each task should have clear success criteria\n\nWHY SPLIT INTO TASKS:\n- Easier to track progress\n- Can resume if interrupted\n- Better error handling (failure of one task doesn't affect others)\n- Parallel work possible in future\n\nAVAILABLE TOOLS (use exact XML format):\n- <createPlan><title>Plan Title</title><instructions>High-level goal and context</instructions></createPlan> - Create the plan FIRST\n- <createTask><title>Task Title</title><instruction>Detailed step-by-step instruction for the model to follow when executing this task</instruction></createTask> - Add tasks AFTER creating plan\n- <updateTask><id>taskId</id><status>pending|completed|blocked</status></updateTask> - Update task status\n- <deleteTask><id>taskId</id></deleteTask> - Remove a task\n- <viewTask/> or <viewTask><id>taskId</id></viewTask> - View plan or specific task\n- <listTasks/> - List all tasks in current plan\n- <TreeView><path>.</path><depth>3</depth></TreeView> - Show directory tree. Params: [<path>], [<depth>] (default 3), [<pattern>] (glob filter), [<showHidden>]\n\nTOOL USAGE GUIDELINES:\n- Terminal: Use ONLY for one-liner commands. For complex scripts or data processing, use WriteFile/CreateFile.\n- WriteFile / CreateFile: Use for content < 2048 bytes in one call, or when creating a file from scratch.\n- AppendFile: Use when content > 2048 bytes (write first chunk with WriteFile, then AppendFile for rest). Also use for adding new content to existing files \u2014 avoids rewriting the whole file.\n- ReplaceLine: Use for targeted line edits. Specify a single line or a range of lines to replace with new content. Prefer this over WriteFile when you only need to change specific lines.\n  **CRITICAL ReplaceLine rules:**\n  - Always ReadFile first to count lines and get exact line numbers (1-indexed)\n  - When replacing a block (CSS rule, function, class), include BOTH the opening AND closing delimiters in the range\n  - Example: to replace a block on lines 15-22, set fromLine=15, toLine=22\n  - After ReplaceLine, use ReadFile to verify the result looks correct\n  - If unsure about line range, replace fewer lines and iterate\n- TreeView: Use to explore project directory structure. Set depth=0 for unlimited depth.\n- General Rule: NEVER call multiple tool calls for large content. Split large data: WriteFile first chunk -> AppendFile remaining.\n- Grep / Find / List / TreeView: Prefer these XML tools over Terminal commands (grep, find, ls).\n- XML Content: Never use backslashes to escape characters inside XML values \u2014 the parser handles special characters natively. Write raw content without escaping quotes (write `\"Hello\"` not `\"Hello\"`).\n- EDITING MINDSET: Just as planning splits a big job into small focused tasks, split big file writes into small targeted edits. Use ReplaceLine for specific line changes and AppendFile for additions instead of rewriting entire files with WriteFile. Targeted edits are more precise, safer, and preserve previously written content.\n\nEXAMPLE WORKFLOW:\n1. User says: \"I want a web app with login and dashboard\"\n2. You FIRST create the plan:\n   <createPlan><title>Web App Development</title><instructions>Create a web application with user authentication (login) and a dashboard for logged-in users.</instructions></createPlan>\n3. Then you create tasks:\n   <createTask><title>Setup Project Structure</title><instruction>Create project folder with basic files: index.html, style.css, app.js, server.py. Initialize npm if needed.</instruction></createTask>\n   <createTask><title>Create Backend API</title><instruction>Create server.py with Flask/FastAPI. Add login endpoint /api/login that validates username/password and returns JWT token. Add /api/dashboard endpoint that requires auth.</instruction></createTask>\n   <createTask><title>Build Frontend Login</title><instruction>Create index.html with login form. Connect to /api/login. Store JWT token in localStorage. Redirect to dashboard on success.</instruction></createTask>\n   <createTask><title>Build Dashboard</title><instruction>Create dashboard view. Fetch user data from /api/dashboard with token. Display user info and logout button.</instruction></createTask>\n\nWhen all tasks are created, tell the user \"Plan is ready! Type !MODE build to start BUILD mode.\"\n", "sessionId": 202, "rowId": 0, "timestamp": 1782968151.7400355, "date": "2026-07-02"} -->

## [05:01] SYSTEM

> You are in BUILD MODE. You are code agent. Your role is to execute the tasks created in plan mode.
> 
> MODE: BUILD (Thinking ENABLED - you can reason step by step)
> 
> IMPORTANT WORKFLOW:
> 1. You will receive tasks automatically (from plan mode). Execute each task using available tools.
> 2. If you created your own tasks in build mode, call <planDone/> to start executing the first task.
> 3. MANDATORY PROGRESS REPORTING: After completing any meaningful step, call <LogProgress><taskId>TASK_ID</taskId><what...
> (truncated, 8516 chars total)

<!-- {"role": "system", "content": "\nYou are in BUILD MODE. You are code agent. Your role is to execute the tasks created in plan mode.\n\nMODE: BUILD (Thinking ENABLED - you can reason step by step)\n\nIMPORTANT WORKFLOW:\n1. You will receive tasks automatically (from plan mode). Execute each task using available tools.\n2. If you created your own tasks in build mode, call <planDone/> to start executing the first task.\n3. MANDATORY PROGRESS REPORTING: After completing any meaningful step, call <LogProgress><taskId>TASK_ID</taskId><whatWasDone>Specific action completed</whatWasDone></LogProgress>\n4. MANDATORY SELF-VERIFICATION: Before calling <nextTask>completed</nextTask>, verify your work:\n   - If you wrote code: verify it runs or read it back with ReadFile\n   - If you made edits: verify changes with ReadFile\n   - If you created files: confirm they exist with List or TreeView\n   - If you deleted files: confirm they no longer exist\n5. When a task is verified completed, call <nextTask>completed</nextTask>\n6. If blocked, call <nextTask>blocked</nextTask> with detailed explanation\n7. When all tasks done, call <jobDone/> to finish the plan\n\nBLOCKED TASK HANDLING:\nWhen you encounter a blocker:\n1. Call <LogProgress><taskId>ID</taskId><whatWasDone>Attempted X, blocked because Y</whatWasDone></LogProgress>\n2. Call <nextTask>blocked</nextTask> and explain EXACTLY:\n   - What you tried to do\n   - What blocked you (error message, missing file, etc.)\n   - What specific information or action is needed to unblock\n   - What the user should do or provide\n\nAVAILABLE TOOLS (use exact XML format):\n- <Terminal><arg1>ls</arg1><arg2>-l</arg2></Terminal>: Execute terminal commands. Use ONLY for one-liner commands. Params: <arg1>, [<arg2>], ... (dynamic args)\n- <ReadFile><fileName>README.md</fileName></ReadFile>: Read file. Params: <fileName>\n- <WriteFile><fileName>README.md</fileName><contentOfFile># Simple hello world app.</contentOfFile></WriteFile>: Write file. Use for content < 4096 bytes. For larger content, use WriteFile for first chunk then AppendFile. Params: <fileName>, <contentOfFile>\n- <AppendFile><fileName>README.md</fileName><contentOfFile># Second line</contentOfFile><fromLineNumber>1</fromLineNumber></AppendFile>: Append to file. Use for content > 4096 bytes or adding to existing files. Params: <fileName>, <contentOfFile>, [<fromLineNumber>]\n- <CreateFile><fileName>testfile.sh</fileName><contentOfFile># new content</contentOfFile></CreateFile>: Create new file (fails if exists). If file exists and you want to overwrite, use WriteFile instead. Params: <fileName>, <contentOfFile>\n- <List><path>.</path></List>: List files. Prefer this over Terminal ls. Params: [<path>] (optional)\n- <listTools/>: Show all tools. No params.\n- <TreeView><path>.</path><depth>3</depth></TreeView>: Show directory tree. Explore project structure, set depth=0 for unlimited. Params: [<path>], [<depth>] (default 3), [<pattern>] (glob filter), [<showHidden>]\n- <ExecuteScript><fileName>ls</fileName><args>-l</args></ExecuteScript>: Run script (.py, .sh, .js, etc). Params: <fileName>, [<args>]\n- <Grep><pattern>search_term</pattern><fileName>file.txt</fileName><recursive>true</recursive></Grep>: Search by regex. Prefer this over Terminal grep. Params: <pattern>, [<fileName>], [<recursive>]\n- <Diff><file1>file1.txt</file1><file2>file2.txt</file2><unified>3</unified></Diff>: Compare files. Params: <file1>, <file2>, [<unified>]\n- <Sed><pattern>old_text</pattern><replacement>new_text</replacement><fileName>file.txt</fileName><inplace>true</inplace></Sed>: Find/replace. Params: <pattern>, <replacement>, <fileName>, [<inplace>]\n- <ReplaceLine><fileName>file.txt</fileName><fromLine>10</fromLine><toLine>20</toLine><replacement>new content</replacement></ReplaceLine>: Replace specific line(s) in a file. Use for targeted edits instead of rewriting the whole file. Params: <fileName>, <fromLine> (required), [<toLine>] (optional, defaults to fromLine), <replacement>\n  **CRITICAL: Always ReadFile first to get correct line numbers. When replacing a block, include its opening AND closing delimiters in the range. After ReplaceLine, ReadFile to verify.\n- <Find><pattern>*.py</pattern><path>.</path></Find>: Find by name. Prefer this over Terminal find. Params: <pattern>, [<path>]\n- <Head><fileName>file.txt</fileName><lines>10</lines></Head>: First N lines. Params: <fileName>, [<lines>]\n- <Tail><fileName>file.txt</fileName><lines>10</lines></Tail>: Last N lines. Params: <fileName>, [<lines>]\n- <Sort><fileName>file.txt</fileName><numeric>true</numeric></Sort>: Sort lines. Params: <fileName>, [<numeric>], [<reverse>], [<unique>]\n\nPLAN MANAGEMENT TOOLS (use these to track progress):\n- <planDone/> - Signal planning is done, start the first pending task\n- <nextTask>completed</nextTask> - Mark current task completed, get next task\n- <nextTask>blocked</nextTask> - Mark current task blocked, explain why\n- <LogProgress><taskId>task_id</taskId><whatWasDone>What you did</whatWasDone></LogProgress> - Log progress on current task\n- <viewTask/> - View current plan and tasks\n- <listTasks/> - List all tasks\n- <jobDone/> - Finish the plan (only when all tasks are done or you want to end early)\n- <createPlan><title>Plan Title</title><instructions>Goal description</instructions></createPlan> - Create a new plan (replaces current). Use when current plan needs full replacement.\n- <createTask><title>Task Title</title><instruction>What to do</instruction></createTask> - Add a new task to the current plan. Always create a plan first.\n- <updateTask><taskId>id</taskId><title>New Title</title><instruction>New instruction</instruction></updateTask> - Update a task's title and/or instruction.\n- <deleteTask><taskId>id</taskId></deleteTask> - Remove a task from the current plan.\n- <deletePlan/> - Delete the current plan entirely.\n- <deleteDraft/> - Delete the unsaved draft plan.\n- <deleteAllPlans/> - Delete all plans.\n\nTOOL USAGE RULES:\n- NEVER call multiple tool calls for large content. Split large data: WriteFile first chunk -> AppendFile remaining.\n- Prefer targeted edits: Use ReplaceLine for specific line changes and AppendFile for additions instead of rewriting entire files with WriteFile. This is more precise and preserves unrelated content.\n- Prefer XML tools (Grep, Find, List) over Terminal commands (grep, find, ls).\n- For file manipulation with complex data, use WriteFile/AppendFile. For one-liners, echo/cat/tee with Terminal is fine.\n- Use ExecuteScript to run scripts you create (WriteFile/CreateFile). Terminal is for system binaries only.\n- Save useful commands and solutions as tips with <SaveTip>. Retrieve them with <GetTip>. Browse with <ListTips>. Bring saved tips into context with <ReinsertTip>.\n- XML Content: Never use backslashes to escape characters inside XML values \u2014 the parser handles special characters natively. Write raw content without escaping quotes (write `\"Hello\"` not `\"Hello\"`).\n\nEXAMPLE WORKFLOW (tasks from plan mode):\n1. Task received: \"Create project folder with basic files\"\n2. Use Terminal to create folder: mkdir myproject\n3. Use WriteFile/CreateFile to create index.html, style.css, app.js\n4. Call <LogProgress><taskId>1</taskId><whatWasDone>Created project folder with 3 files</whatWasDone></LogProgress>\n5. Read back files with ReadFile to verify content is correct\n6. Call <nextTask>completed</nextTask>\n7. Next task is received automatically\n8. Repeat until all tasks done\n9. Call <jobDone/> when finished\n\nEXAMPLE WORKFLOW (self-created tasks in build mode):\n1. Create plan and tasks with createPlan + createTask\n2. Call <planDone/> to start the first pending task\n3. Execute the task using available tools\n4. Call <LogProgress><taskId>ID</taskId><whatWasDone>What was accomplished</whatWasDone></LogProgress>\n5. Verify work with ReadFile/List/TreeView\n6. Call <nextTask>completed</nextTask> when done\n7. Repeat until all tasks done\n8. Call <jobDone/> when finished\n\nBLOCKED EXAMPLE:\n1. Task: \"Install dependency X\"\n2. Attempt: <Terminal><arg1>pip</arg1><arg2>install</arg2><arg3>package-that-does-not-exist</arg3></Terminal>\n3. Error: \"Package not found\"\n4. <LogProgress><taskId>3</taskId><whatWasDone>Attempted to install package-that-does-not-exist, failed with error: Package not found</whatWasDone></LogProgress>\n5. <nextTask>blocked</nextTask>: \"Tried to install package-that-does-not-exist via pip but got error 'Package not found'. Need to verify correct package name or install from alternative source. User should provide correct package name or installation method.\"\n", "sessionId": 202, "rowId": 2, "timestamp": 1782968480.7400327, "date": "2026-07-02"} -->

Your role is to analyze user requests and create structured task plans.\n\nMODE: PLAN (Thinking ENABLED)\n\nIMPORTANT WORKFLOW:\n\nPHASE 0 - CONTEXT GATHERING (MANDATORY):\nBefore creating ANY plan, you MUST understand the existing codebase:\n1. The user may provide files to read directly.\n\nPHASE 1 - CREATE PLAN:\nCall <createPlan><title>Plan Title</title><instructions>High-level goal description</instructions></createPlan>\n\nPHASE 2 - CREATE TASKS:\nCall <createTask><title>Task Title</title><instruction>Detailed instruction for this task</instruction></createTask> for each step\n\nPHASE 3 - FINALIZE:\nWhen all tasks are created, tell user: \"Plan is ready! Type !MODE build to start BUILD mode.\"\n\nHOW TO SPLIT USER INSTRUCTIONS INTO TASKS:\n1. Analyze the user's goal - what is the end result they want?\n2. Identify distinct steps that can be done independently\n3. Create tasks for each step with clear, actionable instructions\n4. Order matters - earlier tasks should enable later ones\n5. Be specific - each task should have a clear beginning and end\n\nTASK SIZE GUIDELINES (CRITICAL):\n- Each task should be completable in 1-5 minutes of AI work\n- A task represents ONE logical unit (e.g., \"Create login form\" not \"Build entire auth system\")\n- If a task requires >3 file edits, split it into smaller tasks\n- Tasks should be independently verifiable\n- Prefer 5-10 small tasks over 1-2 large ones\n- Each task should have clear success criteria\n\nWHY SPLIT INTO TASKS:\n- Easier to track progress\n- Can resume if interrupted\n- Better error handling (failure of one task doesn't affect others)\n- Parallel work possible in future\n\nAVAILABLE TOOLS (use exact XML format):\n- <createPlan><title>Plan Title</title><instructions>High-level goal and context</instructions></createPlan> - Create the plan FIRST\n- <createTask><title>Task Title</title><instruction>Detailed step-by-step instruction for the model to follow when executing this task</instruction></createTask> - Add tasks AFTER creating plan\n- <updateTask><id>taskId</id><status>pending|completed|blocked</status></updateTask> - Update task status\n- <deleteTask><id>taskId</id></deleteTask> - Remove a task\n- <viewTask/> or <viewTask><id>taskId</id></viewTask> - View plan or specific task\n- <listTasks/> - List all tasks in current plan\n- <TreeView><path>.</path><depth>3</depth></TreeView> - Show directory tree. Params: [<path>], [<depth>] (default 3), [<pattern>] (glob filter), [<showHidden>]\n\nTOOL USAGE GUIDELINES:\n- Terminal: Use ONLY for one-liner commands. For complex scripts or data processing, use WriteFile/CreateFile.\n- WriteFile / CreateFile: Use for content < 2048 bytes in one call, or when creating a file from scratch.\n- AppendFile: Use when content > 2048 bytes (write first chunk with WriteFile, then AppendFile for rest). Also use for adding new content to existing files \u2014 avoids rewriting the whole file.\n- ReplaceLine: Use for targeted line edits. Specify a single line or a range of lines to replace with new content. Prefer this over WriteFile when you only need to change specific lines.\n  **CRITICAL ReplaceLine rules:**\n  - Always ReadFile first to count lines and get exact line numbers (1-indexed)\n  - When replacing a block (CSS rule, function, class), include BOTH the opening AND closing delimiters in the range\n  - Example: to replace a block on lines 15-22, set fromLine=15, toLine=22\n  - After ReplaceLine, use ReadFile to verify the result looks correct\n  - If unsure about line range, replace fewer lines and iterate\n- TreeView: Use to explore project directory structure. Set depth=0 for unlimited depth.\n- General Rule: NEVER call multiple tool calls for large content. Split large data: WriteFile first chunk -> AppendFile remaining.\n- Grep / Find / List / TreeView: Prefer these XML tools over Terminal commands (grep, find, ls).\n- XML Content: Never use backslashes to escape characters inside XML values \u2014 the parser handles special characters natively. Write raw content without escaping quotes (write `\"Hello\"` not `\"Hello\"`).\n- EDITING MINDSET: Just as planning splits a big job into small focused tasks, split big file writes into small targeted edits. Use ReplaceLine for specific line changes and AppendFile for additions instead of rewriting entire files with WriteFile. Targeted edits are more precise, safer, and preserve previously written content.\n\nEXAMPLE WORKFLOW:\n1. User says: \"I want a web app with login and dashboard\"\n2. You FIRST create the plan:\n   <createPlan><title>Web App Development</title><instructions>Create a web application with user authentication (login) and a dashboard for logged-in users.</instructions></createPlan>\n3. Then you create tasks:\n   <createTask><title>Setup Project Structure</title><instruction>Create project folder with basic files: index.html, style.css, app.js, server.py. Initialize npm if needed.</instruction></createTask>\n   <createTask><title>Create Backend API</title><instruction>Create server.py with Flask/FastAPI. Add login endpoint /api/login that validates username/password and returns JWT token. Add /api/dashboard endpoint that requires auth.</instruction></createTask>\n   <createTask><title>Build Frontend Login</title><instruction>Create index.html with login form. Connect to /api/login. Store JWT token in localStorage. Redirect to dashboard on success.</instruction></createTask>\n   <createTask><title>Build Dashboard</title><instruction>Create dashboard view. Fetch user data from /api/dashboard with token. Display user info and logout button.</instruction></createTask>\n\nWhen all tasks are created, tell the user \"Plan is ready! Type !MODE build to start BUILD mode.\"\n", "sessionId": 204, "rowId": 0, "timestamp": 1782969592.3561358, "date": "2026-07-02"} -->

<!-- {"role": "system", "content": "\nYou are in BUILD MODE. You are code agent. Your role is to execute the tasks created in plan mode.\n\nMODE: BUILD (Thinking ENABLED - you can reason step by step)\n\nIMPORTANT WORKFLOW:\n1. You will receive tasks automatically (from plan mode). Execute each task using available tools.\n2. If you created your own tasks in build mode, call <planDone/> to start executing the first task.\n3. MANDATORY PROGRESS REPORTING: After completing any meaningful step, call <LogProgress><taskId>TASK_ID</taskId><whatWasDone>Specific action completed</whatWasDone></LogProgress>\n4. MANDATORY SELF-VERIFICATION: Before calling <nextTask>completed</nextTask>, verify your work:\n   - If you wrote code: verify it runs or read it back with ReadFile\n   - If you made edits: verify changes with ReadFile\n   - If you created files: confirm they exist with List or TreeView\n   - If you deleted files: confirm they no longer exist\n5. When a task is verified completed, call <nextTask>completed</nextTask>\n6. If blocked, call <nextTask>blocked</nextTask> with detailed explanation\n7. When all tasks done, call <jobDone/> to finish the plan\n\nBLOCKED TASK HANDLING:\nWhen you encounter a blocker:\n1. Call <LogProgress><taskId>ID</taskId><whatWasDone>Attempted X, blocked because Y</whatWasDone></LogProgress>\n2. Call <nextTask>blocked</nextTask> and explain EXACTLY:\n   - What you tried to do\n   - What blocked you (error message, missing file, etc.)\n   - What specific information or action is needed to unblock\n   - What the user should do or provide\n\nAVAILABLE TOOLS (use exact XML format):\n- <Terminal><arg1>ls</arg1><arg2>-l</arg2></Terminal>: Execute terminal commands. Use ONLY for one-liner commands. Params: <arg1>, [<arg2>], ... (dynamic args)\n- <ReadFile><fileName>README.md</fileName></ReadFile>: Read file. Params: <fileName>\n- <WriteFile><fileName>README.md</fileName><contentOfFile># Simple hello world app.</contentOfFile></WriteFile>: Write file. Use for content < 4096 bytes. For larger content, use WriteFile for first chunk then AppendFile. Params: <fileName>, <contentOfFile>\n- <AppendFile><fileName>README.md</fileName><contentOfFile># Second line</contentOfFile><fromLineNumber>1</fromLineNumber></AppendFile>: Append to file. Use for content > 4096 bytes or adding to existing files. Params: <fileName>, <contentOfFile>, [<fromLineNumber>]\n- <CreateFile><fileName>testfile.sh</fileName><contentOfFile># new content</contentOfFile></CreateFile>: Create new file (fails if exists). If file exists and you want to overwrite, use WriteFile instead. Params: <fileName>, <contentOfFile>\n- <List><path>.</path></List>: List files. Prefer this over Terminal ls. Params: [<path>] (optional)\n- <listTools/>: Show all tools. No params.\n- <TreeView><path>.</path><depth>3</depth></TreeView>: Show directory tree. Explore project structure, set depth=0 for unlimited. Params: [<path>], [<depth>] (default 3), [<pattern>] (glob filter), [<showHidden>]\n- <ExecuteScript><fileName>ls</fileName><args>-l</args></ExecuteScript>: Run script (.py, .sh, .js, etc). Params: <fileName>, [<args>]\n- <Grep><pattern>search_term</pattern><fileName>file.txt</fileName><recursive>true</recursive></Grep>: Search by regex. Prefer this over Terminal grep. Params: <pattern>, [<fileName>], [<recursive>]\n- <Diff><file1>file1.txt</file1><file2>file2.txt</file2><unified>3</unified></Diff>: Compare files. Params: <file1>, <file2>, [<unified>]\n- <Sed><pattern>old_text</pattern><replacement>new_text</replacement><fileName>file.txt</fileName><inplace>true</inplace></Sed>: Find/replace. Params: <pattern>, <replacement>, <fileName>, [<inplace>]\n- <ReplaceLine><fileName>file.txt</fileName><fromLine>10</fromLine><toLine>20</toLine><replacement>new content</replacement></ReplaceLine>: Replace specific line(s) in a file. Use for targeted edits instead of rewriting the whole file. Params: <fileName>, <fromLine> (required), [<toLine>] (optional, defaults to fromLine), <replacement>\n  **CRITICAL: Always ReadFile first to get correct line numbers. When replacing a block, include its opening AND closing delimiters in the range. After ReplaceLine, ReadFile to verify.\n- <Find><pattern>*.py</pattern><path>.</path></Find>: Find by name. Prefer this over Terminal find. Params: <pattern>, [<path>]\n- <Head><fileName>file.txt</fileName><lines>10</lines></Head>: First N lines. Params: <fileName>, [<lines>]\n- <Tail><fileName>file.txt</fileName><lines>10</lines></Tail>: Last N lines. Params: <fileName>, [<lines>]\n- <Sort><fileName>file.txt</fileName><numeric>true</numeric></Sort>: Sort lines. Params: <fileName>, [<numeric>], [<reverse>], [<unique>]\n\nPLAN MANAGEMENT TOOLS (use these to track progress):\n- <planDone/> - Signal planning is done, start the first pending task\n- <nextTask>completed</nextTask> - Mark current task completed, get next task\n- <nextTask>blocked</nextTask> - Mark current task blocked, explain why\n- <LogProgress><taskId>task_id</taskId><whatWasDone>What you did</whatWasDone></LogProgress> - Log progress on current task\n- <viewTask/> - View current plan and tasks\n- <listTasks/> - List all tasks\n- <jobDone/> - Finish the plan (only when all tasks are done or you want to end early)\n- <createPlan><title>Plan Title</title><instructions>Goal description</instructions></createPlan> - Create a new plan (replaces current). Use when current plan needs full replacement.\n- <createTask><title>Task Title</title><instruction>What to do</instruction></createTask> - Add a new task to the current plan. Always create a plan first.\n- <updateTask><taskId>id</taskId><title>New Title</title><instruction>New instruction</instruction></updateTask> - Update a task's title and/or instruction.\n- <deleteTask><taskId>id</taskId></deleteTask> - Remove a task from the current plan.\n- <deletePlan/> - Delete the current plan entirely.\n- <deleteDraft/> - Delete the unsaved draft plan.\n- <deleteAllPlans/> - Delete all plans.\n\nTOOL USAGE RULES:\n- NEVER call multiple tool calls for large content. Split large data: WriteFile first chunk -> AppendFile remaining.\n- Prefer targeted edits: Use ReplaceLine for specific line changes and AppendFile for additions instead of rewriting entire files with WriteFile. This is more precise and preserves unrelated content.\n- Prefer XML tools (Grep, Find, List) over Terminal commands (grep, find, ls).\n- For file manipulation with complex data, use WriteFile/AppendFile. For one-liners, echo/cat/tee with Terminal is fine.\n- Use ExecuteScript to run scripts you create (WriteFile/CreateFile). Terminal is for system binaries only.\n- Save useful commands and solutions as tips with <SaveTip>. Retrieve them with <GetTip>. Browse with <ListTips>. Bring saved tips into context with <ReinsertTip>.\n- XML Content: Never use backslashes to escape characters inside XML values \u2014 the parser handles special characters natively. Write raw content without escaping quotes (write `\"Hello\"` not `\"Hello\"`).\n\nEXAMPLE WORKFLOW (tasks from plan mode):\n1. Task received: \"Create project folder with basic files\"\n2. Use Terminal to create folder: mkdir myproject\n3. Use WriteFile/CreateFile to create index.html, style.css, app.js\n4. Call <LogProgress><taskId>1</taskId><whatWasDone>Created project folder with 3 files</whatWasDone></LogProgress>\n5. Read back files with ReadFile to verify content is correct\n6. Call <nextTask>completed</nextTask>\n7. Next task is received automatically\n8. Repeat until all tasks done\n9. Call <jobDone/> when finished\n\nEXAMPLE WORKFLOW (self-created tasks in build mode):\n1. Create plan and tasks with createPlan + createTask\n2. Call <planDone/> to start the first pending task\n3. Execute the task using available tools\n4. Call <LogProgress><taskId>ID</taskId><whatWasDone>What was accomplished</whatWasDone></LogProgress>\n5. Verify work with ReadFile/List/TreeView\n6. Call <nextTask>completed</nextTask> when done\n7. Repeat until all tasks done\n8. Call <jobDone/> when finished\n\nBLOCKED EXAMPLE:\n1. Task: \"Install dependency X\"\n2. Attempt: <Terminal><arg1>pip</arg1><arg2>install</arg2><arg3>package-that-does-not-exist</arg3></Terminal>\n3. Error: \"Package not found\"\n4. <LogProgress><taskId>3</taskId><whatWasDone>Attempted to install package-that-does-not-exist, failed with error: Package not found</whatWasDone></LogProgress>\n5. <nextTask>blocked</nextTask>: \"Tried to install package-that-does-not-exist via pip but got error 'Package not found'. Need to verify correct package name or install from alternative source. User should provide correct package name or installation method.\"\n", "sessionId": 204, "rowId": 1, "timestamp": 1782969646.060839, "date": "2026-07-02"} -->

# LevelDB Socket Server
> 
> A threaded Python socket server providing a MySQL-like command interface over LevelDB backend.
> 
> ## Features
> 
> - **Threaded TCP Socket Server** - Handles multiple concurrent clients
> - **Authentication** - Simple username/password (admin/skrlat)
> - **LevelDB Backend** - Persistent key-value storage with table namespacing
> - **SQL-like Commands** - CREATE, DROP, INSERT, SELECT, UPDATE, DELETE
> - **Netcat Compatible** - Test with standard netcat client
> 
> ## Installation
> 
> ```bash
> ...

## [00:05] tool: ReadFile
"""
> Command Execution Framework for LevelDB Socket Server
> """
> 
> from typing import Dict, Any, Optional, List
> from database import Database
> 
> 
> class Command:
>     def __init__(self, db: Database):
>         self.db = db
>     
>     def execute(self, params: Dict[str, Any], client_state: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
>         raise NotImplementedError
>     
>     def validate_params(self, params: Dict[str, Any], required: List[str]) -> bool:
>         for param in required:
>             if param not in params or param...
> (truncated, 8306 chars total)

<!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "\"\"\"\nCommand Execution Framework for LevelDB Socket Server\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom typing import Dict, Any, Optional, List\nfrom database import Database\n\n\nclass Command:\n    def __init__(self, db: Database):\n        self.db = db\n    \n    def execute(self, params: Dict[str, Any], client_state: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:\n        raise NotImplementedError\n    \n    def validate_params(self, params: Dict[str, Any], required: List[str]) -> bool:\n        for param in required:\n            if param not in params or params[param] is None:\n                return False\n        return True\n\n\nclass CreateDatabaseCommand(Command):\n    def execute(self, params, client_state):\n        if not self.validate_params(params, ['database']):\n            return \"ERROR: Database name required\"\n        try:\n            self.db.create_database(params['database'])\n            return f\"OK: Database '{params['database']}' created\"\n        except Exception as e:\n            return f\"ERROR: {e}\"\n\n\nclass DropDatabaseCommand(Command):\n    def execute(self, params, client_state):\n        if not self.validate_params(params, ['database']):\n            return \"ERROR: Database name required\"\n        try:\n            self.db.drop_database(params['database'])\n            if client_state.get('current_db') == params['database']:\n                client_state['current_db'] = None\n            return f\"OK: Database '{params['database']}' dropped\"\n        except Exception as e:\n            return f\"ERROR: {e}\"\n\n\nclass UseDatabaseCommand(Command):\n    def execute(self, params, client_state):\n        if not self.validate_params(params, ['database']):\n            return \"ERROR: Database name required\"\n        try:\n            result = self.db.use_database(params['database'])\n            client_state['current_db'] = params['database']\n            return result\n        except Exception as e:\n            return f\"ERROR: {e}\"\n\n\nclass CreateTableCommand(Command):\n    def execute(self, params, client_state):\n        if not self.validate_params(params, ['table']):\n            return \"ERROR: Table name required\"\n        if not client_state.get('current_db'):\n            return \"ERROR: No database selected\"\n        try:\n            columns = params.get('columns', [])\n            self.db.create_table(params['table'], columns)\n            return f\"OK: Table '{params['table']}' created\"\n        except Exception as e:\n            return f\"ERROR: {e}\"\n\n\nclass DropTableCommand(Command):\n    def execute(self, params, client_state):\n        if not self.validate_params(params, ['table']):\n            return \"ERROR: Table name required\"\n        if not client_state.get('current_db'):\n            return \"ERROR: No database selected\"\n        try:\n            self.db.drop_table(params['table'])\n            return f\"OK: Table '{params['table']}' dropped\"\n        except Exception as e:\n            return f\"ERROR: {e}\"\n\n\nclass InsertCommand(Command):\n    def execute(self, params, client_state):\n        if not self.validate_params(params, ['table', 'values']):\n            return \"ERROR: Table and values required\"\n        if not client_state.get('current_db'):\n            return \"ERROR: No database selected\"\n        try:\n            self.db.insert(params['table'], params['values'])\n            return f\"OK: Inserted into '{params['table']}'\"\n        except Exception as e:\n            return f\"ERROR: {e}\"\n\n\nclass SelectCommand(Command):\n    def execute(self, params, client_state):\n        if not self.validate_params(params, ['table']):\n            return \"ERROR: Table name required\"\n        if not client_state.get('current_db'):\n            return \"ERROR: No database selected\"\n        try:\n            columns = params.get('columns', ['*'])\n            where = params.get('where')\n            order_by = params.get('order_by')\n            order_desc = params.get('order_desc', False)\n            result = self.db.select(params['table'], columns, where, order_by, order_desc)\n            return result\n        except Exception as e:\n            return f\"ERROR: {e}\"\n\n\nclass UpdateCommand(Command):\n    def execute(self, params, client_state):\n        if not self.validate_params(params, ['table', 'set']):\n            return \"ERROR: Table and SET required\"\n        if not client_state.get('current_db'):\n            return \"ERROR: No database selected\"\n        try:\n            count = self.db.update(params['table'], params['set'], params.get('where'))\n            return f\"OK: Updated {count} row(s)\"\n        except Exception as e:\n            return f\"ERROR: {e}\"\n\n\nclass DeleteCommand(Command):\n    def execute(self, params, client_state):\n        if not self.validate_params(params, ['table']):\n            return \"ERROR: Table name required\"\n        if not client_state.get('current_db'):\n            return \"ERROR: No database selected\"\n        try:\n            count = self.db.delete(params['table'], params.get('where'))\n            return f\"OK: Deleted {count} row(s)\"\n        except Exception as e:\n            return f\"ERROR: {e}\"\n\n\nclass ShowTablesCommand(Command):\n    def execute(self, params, client_state):\n        if not client_state.get('current_db'):\n            return \"ERROR: No database selected\"\n        try:\n            tables = self.db.list_tables()\n            return \"OK:\\n\" + \"\\n\".join(tables) if tables else \"OK: No tables\"\n        except Exception as e:\n            return f\"ERROR: {e}\"\n\n\nclass ShowDatabasesCommand(Command):\n    def execute(self, params, client_state):\n        try:\n            dbs = self.db.list_databases()\n            return \"OK:\\n\" + \"\\n\".join(dbs) if dbs else \"OK: No databases\"\n        except Exception as e:\n            return f\"ERROR: {e}\"\n\n\nclass ShowUsersCommand(Command):\n    def execute(self, params, client_state):\n        if not client_state.get('is_admin'):\n            return \"ERROR: Admin only\"\n        try:\n            users = self.db.list_users()\n            return \"OK:\\n\" + \"\\n\".join(users) if users else \"OK: No users\"\n        except Exception as e:\n            return f\"ERROR: {e}\"\n\n\nclass HelpCommand(Command):\n    def execute(self, params, client_state):\n        is_admin = client_state.get('is_admin', False)\n        help_text = \"\"\"Available commands:\n  SHOW DATABASES           - List databases\n  CREATE DATABASE <name>   - Create database\n  DROP DATABASE <name>     - Delete database\n  USE <database>           - Select database\n  SHOW TABLES              - List tables\n  \n  CREATE TABLE <name> (col [PRIMARY KEY], col [INDEX], ...)\n                           - Create table with indexes\n  DROP TABLE <name>        - Delete table\n  \n  INSERT INTO <t> VALUES (v...)  - Insert row\n  SELECT * FROM <t>              - Select all\n  SELECT * FROM <t> ORDER BY c [ASC|DESC]\n                           - Select sorted\n  SELECT c FROM <t> WHERE cond ORDER BY c\n                           - Select filtered\n  UPDATE <t> SET c=v WHERE...    - Update\n  DELETE FROM <t> WHERE cond     - Delete\n  \n  HELP <!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "\"\"\"\nAuthentication module using database-backed user management\n\"\"\"\n\nimport hashlib\nimport secrets\nfrom typing import Dict, Set, List, Optional, Tuple\nfrom database import Database\n\n\nclass Authenticator:\n    \"\"\"Database-backed authentication with privilege checking\"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, db: Database):\n        self.db = db\n        self.active_sessions: Dict[str, Dict] = {}  # Create session\n        token = secrets.token_hex(16)\n        user_info = {\n            \"username\": username,\n            \"is_admin\": is_admin,\n            \"privileges\": privileges\n        }\n        self.active_sessions[token] = user_info\n        \n        return True, token, user_info\n    \n    def validate_session(self, token: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Check if session token is valid.\"\"\"\n        return token in self.active_sessions\n    \n    def get_user_info(self, token: str) -> Optional[Dict]:\n        \"\"\"Get user info from session token.\"\"\"\n        return self.active_sessions.get(token)\n    \n    def end_session(self, token: str):\n        \"\"\"End a session.\"\"\"\n        if token in self.active_sessions:\n            del self.active_sessions[token]\n    \n    def check_privilege(self, token: str, db_name: str, table_name: str, \n                       required_priv: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Check if user has required privilege.\"\"\"\n        user_info = self.get_user_info(token)\n        if not user_info:\n            return False\n        \n        username = user_info[\"username\"]\n        is_admin = user_info.get(\"is_admin\", False)\n        \n        # Admins have all privileges\n        if is_admin:\n            return True\n        \n        # Check database privileges\n        return self.db.check_privilege(username, db_name, table_name, required_priv)\n    \n    def has_db_access(self, token: str, db_name: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Check if user has any access to database.\"\"\"\n        return self.check_privilege(token, db_name, \"*\", \"CONNECT\")\n    \n    def has_table_access(self, token: str, db_name: str, table_name: str, \n                         operation: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Check if user can perform operation on table.\"\"\"\n        priv_map = {\n            \"SELECT\": \"SELECT\",\n            \"INSERT\": \"INSERT\",\n            \"UPDATE\": \"UPDATE\",\n            \"DELETE\": \"DELETE\",\n            \"CREATE\": \"CREATE\",\n            \"DROP\": \"DROP\"\n        }\n        required_priv = priv_map.get(operation, operation)\n        return self.check_privilege(token, db_name, table_name, required_priv)", "sessionId": 213, "rowId": 0, "timestamp": 1783123534.3039527, "date": "2026-07-04", "name": "ReadFile"} -->

<!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "\"\"\"LevelDB database layer with CRUD operations, user management and privileges.\"\"\"\n\nimport os\nimport json\nimport hashlib\nimport secrets\nimport      prefix = f\"{table_name}:\".encode()\n            for key, value in self._db.iterator(prefix=prefix):\n                if key.startswith(f\"_schema:{table_name}\".encode()):\n                    continue\n                \n                row = json.loads(value.decode())\n                \n                if where:\n                    match = True\n                    for col, val in -> str:\n        \"\"\"Format query results as a table string.\"\"\"\n        if not results:\n            return \"Empty set\"\n        \n        widths = {}\n        for col in columns:\n # LevelDB Socket Server
> 
> A threaded Python socket server providing a MySQL-like command interface over LevelDB backend.
> 
> ## Features
> 
> - **Threaded TCP Socket Server** - Handles multiple concurrent clients
> - **Authentication** - 
> - **LevelDB Backend** - Persistent key-value storage with table namespacing
> - **SQL-like Commands** - CREATE, DROP, INSERT, SELECT, UPDATE, DELETE
> - **Netcat Compatible** - Test with standard netcat client
> 
> ## Installation
> 
> ```bash
> pip install -r requirements.txt
> ```
> 
> ##...

## [04:44] ASSISTANT
Excellent idea! Let me think through the replication architecture before creating a plan.
> 
> ## Replication Architecture Thoughts
> 
> Based on MySQL's approach and LevelDB's characteristics, here's what I recommend:
> 
> ### **Phase 1: Master-Slave Replication** (Start Simple)
> - **One Master**: Accepts all writes, maintains binary log (binlog)
> - **Multiple Slaves**: Replicate from master, can serve reads
> - **Automatic Recovery**: Slaves reconnect and catch up from last known position
> 
> ### **Key Component...
> (truncated, 2321 chars total)

<!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "Excellent idea! Let me think through the replication architecture before creating a plan.\n\n## Replication Architecture Thoughts\n\nBased on MySQL's approach and LevelDB's characteristics, here's what I recommend:\n\n### **Phase 1: Master-Slave Replication** (Start Simple)\n- **One Master**: Accepts all writes, maintains binary log (binlog)\n- **Multiple Slaves**: Replicate from master, can serve reads\n- **Automatic Recovery**: Slaves reconnect and catch up from last known position\n\n### **Key Components:**\n\n1. **Binary Log (Binlog)**\n   - Master logs every write operation (INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE, CREATE, DROP)\n   - Each entry: `[timestamp, server-id, position, database, operation, data]`\n   - Stored in LevelDB for durability\n\n2. **Replication User**\n   - Special user with `REPLICATION SLAVE` privilege\n   - Slave authenticates as this user to master\n\n3. **Replication Protocol**\n   - Slave connects: `REPL CONNECT TO master:port`\n   - Authenticates, then: `REPL STREAM FROM position`\n   - Master streams binlog events continuously\n   - Slave applies events to local database\n\n4. **Configuration**\n   - `--server-id 1` - Unique ID for each server\n   - `--replication-role master|slave` - Server role\n   - `--master-host host:port` - For slaves, master location\n   - `--replication-user user:pass` - Credentials\n\n5. **Recovery**\n   - Slave tracks last received position\n   - On reconnection, requests events from that position\n   - Master maintains binlog history (configurable retention)\n\n### **Commands:**\n```sql\n-- On Master:\nCREATE REPLICATION USER 'repl'@'%' IDENTIFIED BY 'secret';\nGRANT REPLICATION SLAVE ON *.* TO 'repl'@'%';\nSHOW MASTER STATUS; They want:\n\n1. If a server goes down and comes back, it should recover lost data from mirrored servers\n2. When new data is received, it should replicate to other servers\n3. They mentioned MySQL's approach: CREATE USER and GRANT REPLICATION SLAVE\n\nLet me think about this architecture:\n\n**Replication Concepts:**\n- **Master-Slave Replication**: One master writes, slaves replicate and can read\n- **Master-Master Replication**: Multiple masters can write and replicate to each other\n- **Multi-Master**: More complex, conflict resolution needed\n\n**For this LevelDB server, I think we should implement:**\n\n1. **Master-Slave Replication** (simpler to start with):\n   - One master server accepts writes\n   - One or more slave servers replicate from master\n   - Slaves can serve read queries\n   - If master fails, a slave can be promoted\n\n2. **Architecture Components:**\n   - Replication user (special user type with REPLICATION privilege)\n   - Binary log (binlog) - record of all changes\n   - Replication protocol - slaves connect to master and stream changes\n   - Position tracking - Master sends all events from that position\n   - If master was down, slaves can elect new master or wait\n\n7. **Conflict Resolution:**\n   - For master-slave: writes only on master, no conflicts\n   - For multi-master: need conflict resolution (last-write-wins, or custom logic)\n\nI think we should start with **Master-Slave Replication** as it's simpler and covers most use cases. ReplicationClient class (runs on slave):\n   - connect_to_master(host, port, username, password)\n   - send: REPL AUTH user pass\n   - send: REPL STREAM FROM position\n   - receive binlog entries continuously\n   - apply each entry to local database\n\n2. RESET SLAVE - Clear replication state, start from beginning\n4. Slave stores last applied position in LevelDB (data/_slave_state)\n2. On startup, slave reads last position and resumes from there\n3. If connection to master drops:\n   - Retry connection every 5 seconds\n   - On reconnect, request entries from last_applied_position + 1\n4. If master was down and comes back:\n   - Slave automatically reconnects\n   - Catches up on missed entries\n5. Handle network errors gracefully with exponential backoff\n\nAdd to ReplicationClient:\n- save_position(position)\n- load_position() -> returns last saved position\n- reconnect_with_backoff()</instruction></createTask>\n\n<createTask><title>Implement master-master replication (bi-directional)</title><instruction>Extend replication to support master-master:\n\n1. > - --master-host HOST:PORT (for slaves, where to connect)
> - --replication-port PORT (separate port for replication connections)

self.send(response)\n                    if response.startswith(\"ERROR\") or response == \"BYE\":\n                        break\n                    continue\n                \n self.send(\"ERROR: Permission denied\")\n                    continue\n                \n                response = self.commands.execute(cmd_type, params, self.client_state)\n = parts[0].upper()\n        \n        if cmd == \"USER\":\n            if len(parts) < 2:\n                return \"ERROR: Username required\"\n            self.pending_username = parts[1].strip()\n            return \"OK: Send PASS <password>\"\n        \n        elif cmd == \"PASS\":\n            if len(parts) < 2:\n                return \"ERROR: Password required\"\n            if not hasattr(self, 'pending_username'):\n                return \"ERROR: USER first\"\n            \n            password = parts[1].strip()\n            success, token, user_info = self.authenticator.authenticate(\n                self.pending_username, password\n            )\n            \n            if success:\n                self.authenticated = True\n                self.session_token = token\n                self.user_info = user_info\n                self.client_state['username'] = user_info['username']\n                self.client_state['is_admin'] = user_info['is_admin']\n                msg = f\"OK: Welcome {user_info['username']}\"\n                if user_info['is_admin']:\n                    msg += \" (admin)\"\n                return msg + <!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "\"\"\"LevelDB database layer with CRUD operations, user management and privileges.\"\"\"\n\nimport os\nimport json\nimport hashlib\nimport secrets\nimport self._system_db: Optional[plyvel.DB] = None  # For users/privileges\n        self._ensure_data_dir()\n        self._open_system_db()\n    \n    def _ensure_data_dir(self):\n        \"\"\"Ensure data directory exists.\"\"\"\n        if not os.path.exists(self.data_dir):\n            os.makedirs(self.data_dir)\n    \n    def _open_system_db(self):\n        \"\"\"Open system database for users and privileges.\"\"\"\n        system_db_path = os.path.join(self.data_dir, \"_system\")\n        self._system_db = plyvel.DB(system_db_path, create_if_missing=True)\n    \n    def _ensure_system_tables(self):\n        \"\"\"Ensure system tables for users and privileges exist.\"\"\"\n        # Users table\n        if not self._system_db.get(b\"_schema:_users\"):\n            schema = {\"columns\": [\"username\", \"password_hash\", \"is_admin\", \"created_at\"], \"next_id\": 1}\n            self._system_db.put(b\"_schema:_users\", json.dumps(schema).encode())\n        \n        # Privileges table\n        if not self._system_db.get(b\"_schema:_privileges\"):\n            schema = {\"columns\": [\"username\", \"db_pattern\", \"table_pattern\", \"privileges\"], \"next_id\": 1}\n            self._system_db.put(b\"_schema:_privileges\", json.dumps(schema).encode())\n    \n    def _hash_password(self, password: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Hash password using SHA-256 with salt.\"\"\"\n        salt = secrets.token_hex(16)\n        pwdhash = hashlib.sha256((password + salt).encode()).hexdigest()\n        return f\"{salt}${pwdhash}\"\n    \n    def _verify_password(self, password: str, stored_hash: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Verify password against stored hash.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            salt, hash_val = stored_hash.split(\"$\")\n            pwdhash = hashlib.sha256((password + salt).encode()).hexdigest()\n            return pwdhash == hash_val\n        except ValueError:\n            return False\n    \n    def _db_path(self, db_name: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Get path for database directory.\"\"\"\n        return os.path.join(self.data_dir, db_name)\n    \n    def _make_key(self, table_name: str, row_id: str) -> bytes:\n        \"\"\"Create a key for a row.\"\"\"\n        return f\"{table_name}:{row_id}\".encode()\n    \n    def create_database(self, db_name: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Create a new database (LevelDB instance).\"\"\"\n        db_path = self._db_path(db_name)\n        if os.path.exists(db_path):\n            return f\"Database '{db_name}' already exists\"\n        \n        db = plyvel.DB(db_path, create_if_missing=True)\n        db.close()\n        return f\"Database '{db_name}' created successfully\"\n    \n    def drop_database(self, db_name: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Delete a database.\"\"\"\n        db_path = self._db_path(db_name)\n        if not os.path.exists(db_path):\n            return f\"Database '{db_name}' does not exist\"\n        \n        if self.current_db == db_name and self._db:\n            self._db.close()\n            self._db = None\n            self.current_db = None\n        \n        import shutil\n        shutil.rmtree(db_path)\n        return f\"Database '{db_name}' dropped successfully\"\n    \n    def use_database(self, db_name: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Switch to a database.\"\"\"\n        db_path = self._db_path(db_name)\n        if not os.path.exists(db_path):\n            return f\"Database '{db_name}' does not exist\"\n        \n        if self._db:\n            self._db.close()\n        \n        self._db = plyvel.DB(db_path, create_if_missing=True)\n        self.current_db = db_name\n        return f\"Switched to database '{db_name}'\"\n    \n    def create_table(self, table_name: str, columns: List[str], indexes: List[str] = None) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Create a table with optional indexes.\"\"\"\n        if not self._db:\n            return \"No database selected. Use USE <database>\"\n        \n        schema_key = f\"_schema:{table_name}\".encode()\n        if self._db.get(schema_key):\n            return f\"Table '{table_name}' already exists\"\n        \n        parsed_columns = []\n        primary_key = None\n        index_columns = []\n        \n        for col in columns:\n            col_upper = col.upper()\n            if 'PRIMARY KEY' in col_upper:\n                primary_key = col.split()[0]\n                parsed_columns.append(primary_key)\n            elif 'INDEX' in col_upper:\n                idx_col = col.split()[0]\n                parsed_columns.append(idx_col)\n                index_columns.append(idx_col)\n            else:\n                parsed_columns.append(col.strip())\n        \n        schema = {\n            \"columns\": parsed_columns,\n            \"next_id\": 1,\n            \"primary_key\": primary_key,\n            \"indexes\": index_columns\n        }\n        self._db.put(schema_key, json.dumps(schema).encode())\n        \n        if primary_key:\n            idx_key = f\"_index:{table_name}:{primary_key}\".encode()\n            self._db.put(idx_key, json.dumps({}).encode())\n        \n        for idx_col in index_columns:\n            idx_key = f\"_index:{table_name}:{idx_col}\".encode()\n            self._db.put(idx_key, json.dumps({}).encode())\n        \n        return f\"Table '{table_name}' created\"\n    \n    def drop_table(self, table_name: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Drop a table and all its data.\"\"\"\n        if not self._db:\n            return \"No database selected. Use USE <database>\"\n        \n        schema_key = f\"_schema:{table_name}\".encode()\n        if not self._db.get(schema_key):\n            return f\"Table '{table_name}' does not exist\"\n        \n        prefix = f\"{table_name}:\".encode()\n        for key, _ in self._db.iterator(prefix=prefix):\n            self._db.delete(key)\n        \n        self._db.delete(schema_key)\n        return f\"Table '{table_name}' dropped\"\n    \n    def insert(self, table_name: str, values: List[Any]) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Insert a row into a table.\"\"\"\n        if not self._db:\n            return \"No database selected. Use USE <database>\"\n        \n        schema_key = f\"_schema:{table_name}\".encode()\n        schema_data = self._db.get(schema_key)\n        if not schema_data:\n            return f\"Table '{table_name}' does not exist\"\n        \n        schema = json.loads(schema_data.decode())\n        row_id = str(schema[\"next_id\"])\n        \n        row = {\"id\": row_id}\n        for i, col in enumerate(schema[\"columns\"]):\n            if i < len(values):\n                row[col] = values[i]\n        \n        primary_key = schema.get(\"primary_key\")\n        if primary_key and primary_key in row:\n            store_key = str(row[primary_key])\n        else:\n            store_key = row_id\n        \n        key = self._make_key(table_name, store_key)\n        self._db.put(key, json.dumps(row).encode())\n        \n        self._update_indexes(table_name, row, store_key, schema)\n        \n        if not primary_key:\n            schema[\"next_id\"] += 1\n            self._db.put(schema_key, json.dumps(schema).encode())\n        \n        return f\"Inserted 1 row into '{table_name}'\"\n    \n    def _update_indexes(self, table_name: str, row: Dict, row_key: str, schema: Dict):\n        \"\"\"Update all indexes for a row.\"\"\"\n        primary_key = schema.get(\"primary_key\")\n        indexes = schema.get(\"indexes\", [])\n        \n        if primary_key and primary_key in row:\n            idx_key = f\"_index:{table_name}:{primary_key}\".encode()\n            idx_data = self._db.get(idx_key)\n            if idx_data:\n                index_map = json.loads(idx_data.decode())\n                index_map[str(row[primary_key])] = row_key\n                self._db.put(idx_key, json.dumps(index_map).encode())\n        \n        for idx_col in indexes:\n            if idx_col in row:\n                idx_key = f\"_index:{table_name}:{idx_col}\".encode()\n                idx_data = self._db.get(idx_key)\n                if idx_data:\n                    index_map = json.loads(idx_data.decode())\n                    val = str(row[idx_col])\n                    if val not in index_map:\n                        index_map[val] = []\n                    if isinstance(index_map[val], list):\n                        index_map[val].append(row_key)\n                    else:\n                        index_map[val] = [index_map[val], row_key]\n                    self._db.put(idx_key, json.dumps(index_map).encode())\n    \n    def select(self, table_name: str, columns: Optional[List[str]] = None,\n               where: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,\n               order_by: Optional[str] = None,\n               order_desc: bool = False) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Select rows from a table with optional ordering.\"\"\"\n        if not self._db:\n            return \"No database selected. Use USE <database>\"\n        \n        schema_key = f\"_schema:{table_name}\".encode()\n        schema_data = self._db.get(schema_key)\n        if not schema_data:\n            return f\"Table '{table_name}' does not exist\"\n        \n        schema = json.loads(schema_data.decode())\n        if columns is None or \"*\" in columns:\n            columns = [\"id\"] + schema[\"columns\"]\n        \n        results = []\n        \n        if order_by and order_by != \"id\":\n            results = self._select_with_index(table_name, where, order_by, order_desc, schema)\n        else:\n            prefix = f\"{table_name}:\".encode()\n            for key, value in self._db.iterator(prefix=prefix):\n                if key.startswith(f\"_schema:{table_name}\".encode()):\n                    continue\n                \n                row = json.loads(value.decode())\n                \n                if where:\n                    match = True\n                    for col, val in where.items():\n                        if str(row.get(col)) != str(val):\n                            match = False\n                            break\n                    if not match:\n                        continue\n                \n                results.append(row)\n            \n            if order_by == \"id\":\n                results.sort(key=lambda r: r.get(\"id\", \"\"), reverse=order_desc)\n        \n        if not results:\n            return \"Empty set\"\n        \n        filtered_results = []\n        for row in results:\n            filtered_row = {col: row.get(col, \"NULL\") for col in columns}\n            filtered_results.append(filtered_row)\n        \n        return self._format_results(columns, filtered_results)\n    \n    def _select_with_index(self, table_name: str, where: Optional[Dict],\n                          order_by: str, order_desc: bool, schema: Dict) -> List[Dict]:\n        \"\"\"Select using index for ordering.\"\"\"\n        results = []\n        \n        idx_key = f\"_index:{table_name}:{order_by}\".encode()\n        idx_data = self._db.get(idx_key)\n        \n        if idx_data:\n            index_map = json.loads(idx_data.decode())\n            sorted_vals = sorted(index_map.keys(), reverse=order_desc)\n            \n            for val in sorted_vals:\n                row_keys = index_map[val]\n                if not isinstance(row_keys, list):\n                    row_keys = [row_keys]\n                \n                for row_key in row_keys:\n                    row_key_full = f\"{table_name}:{row_key}\".encode()\n                    row_data = self._db.get(row_key_full)\n                    if row_data:\n                        row = json.loads(row_data.decode())\n                        results.append(row)\n        else:\n            prefix = f\"{table_name}:\".encode()\n            for key, value in self._db.iterator(prefix=prefix):\n                if key.startswith(f\"_schema:{table_name}\".encode()):\n                    continue\n                \n                row = json.loads(value.decode())\n                \n                if where:\n                    match = True\n                    for col, val in where.items():\n                        if str(row.get(col)) != str(val):\n                            match = False\n                            break\n                    if not match:\n                        continue\n                \n                results.append(row)\n            \n            results.sort(key=lambda r: r.get(order_by, \"\"), reverse=order_desc)\n        \n        return results\n    \n    def update(self, table_name: str, set_clause: Dict[str, Any],\n               where: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Update rows in a table.\"\"\"\n        if not self._db:\n            return \"No database selected. Use USE <database>\"\n        \n        schema_key = f\"_schema:{table_name}\".encode()\n        schema_data = self._db.get(schema_key)\n        if not schema_data:\n            return f\"Table '{table_name}' does not exist\"\n        \n        schema = json.loads(schema_data.decode())\n        updated = 0\n        prefix = f\"{table_name}:\".encode()\n        \n        for key, value in self._db.iterator(prefix=prefix):\n            if key.startswith(f\"_schema:{table_name}\".encode()):\n                continue\n            \n            row = json.loads(value.decode())\n            \n            if where:\n                match = True\n                for col, val in where.items():\n                    if str(row.get(col)) != str(val):\n                        match = False\n                        break\n                if not match:\n                    continue\n            \n            old_key_val = None\n            primary_key = schema.get(\"primary_key\")\n            if primary_key and primary_key in set_clause:\n                old_key_val = row.get(primary_key)\n            \n            for col, val in set_clause.items():\n                row[col] = val\n            \n            self._db.put(key, json.dumps(row).encode())\n            \n            if old_key_val is not None and primary_key:\n                self._update_indexes(table_name, row, str(row[primary_key]), schema)\n            \n            updated += 1\n        \n        return f\"Updated {updated} row(s) in '{table_name}'\"\n    \n    def delete(self, table_name: str, where: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Delete rows from a table.\"\"\"\n        if not self._db:\n            return \"No database selected. Use USE <database>\"\n        \n        schema_key = f\"_schema:{table_name}\".encode()\n        schema_data = self._db.get(schema_key)\n        if not schema_data:\n            return f\"Table '{table_name}' does not exist\"\n        \n        deleted = 0\n        keys_to_delete = []\n        prefix = f\"{table_name}:\".encode()\n        \n        for key, value in self._db.iterator(prefix=prefix):\n            if key.startswith(f\"_schema:{table_name}\".encode()):\n                continue\n            \n            row = json.loads(value.decode())\n            \n            if where:\n                match = True\n                for col, val in where.items():\n                    if str(row.get(col)) != str(val):\n                        match = False\n                        break\n                if not match:\n                    continue\n            \n            keys_to_delete.append(key)\n        \n        for key in keys_to_delete:\n            self._db.delete(key)\n            deleted += 1\n        \n        return f\"Deleted {deleted} row(s) from '{table_name}'\"\n    \n    def _format_results(self, columns: List[str], results: List[Dict]) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Format query results as a table string.\"\"\"\n        if not results:\n            return \"Empty set\"\n        \n        widths = {}\n        for col in columns:\n            widths[col] = len(col)\n        \n        for row in results:\n            for col in columns:\n                val_str = str(row.get(col, \"NULL\"))\n                widths[col] = max(widths[col], len(val_str))\n        \n        lines = []\n        header = \"| \" + \" | \".join(col.ljust(widths[col]) for col in columns) + \" |\"\n        separator = \"+\" + \"+\".join(\"-\" * (widths[col] + 2) for col in columns) + \"+\"\n        \n        lines.append(separator)\n        lines.append(header)\n        lines.append(separator)\n        \n        for row in results:\n            row_str = \"| \" + \" | \".join(\n                str(row.get(col, \"NULL\")).ljust(widths[col]) for col in columns\n            ) + \" |\"\n            lines.append(row_str)\n        \n        lines.append(separator)\n        lines.append(f\"{len(results)} row(s) in set\")\n        \n        return \"\\n\".join(lines)\n    \n    def close(self):\n        \"\"\"Close the database connection.\"\"\"\n        if self._db:\n            self._db.close()\n            self._db = None\n            self.current_db = None\n        if self._system_db:\n            self._system_db.close()\n            self._system_db = None\n    \n    def list_databases(self) -> List[str]:\n        \"\"\"List all databases in the data directory.\"\"\"\n        if not os.path.exists(self.data_dir):\n            return []\n        \n        databases = []\n        for item in os.listdir(self.data_dir):\n            item_path = os.path.join(self.data_dir, item)\n            if os.path.isdir(item_path) and os.path.exists(os.path.join(item_path, \"CURRENT\")):\n                databases.append(item)\n        \n        return sorted(databases)\n    \n    def list_tables(self) -> List[str]:\n        \"\"\"List all tables in the current database.\"\"\"\n        if not self._db:\n            return []\n        \n        tables = []\n        prefix = b\"_schema:\"\n        \n        for key, _ in self._db.iterator(prefix=prefix):\n            table_name = key.decode().replace(\"_schema:\", \"\")\n            tables.append(table_name)\n        \n        return sorted(tables)\n    \n    def create_user(self, username: str, password: str, is_admin: bool = False) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Create a new user.\"\"\"\n        self._ensure_system_tables()\n        \n        # Check if user exists\n        prefix = b\"_users:\"\n        for key, value in self._system_db.iterator(prefix=prefix):\n            user_data = json.loads(value.decode())\n            if user_data.get(\"username\") == username:\n                return f\"User '{username}' already exists\"\n        \n        # Create user\n        password_hash = self._hash_password(password)\n        user_id = self._get_next_user_id()\n        user_data = {\n            \"id\": user_id,\n            \"username\": username,\n            \"password_hash\": password_hash,\n            \"is_admin\": is_admin,\n            \"created_at\": str(os.times().system)\n        }\n        \n        key = f\"_users:{user_id}\".encode()\n        self._system_db.put(key, json.dumps(user_data).encode())\n        return f\"User '{username}' created successfully\"\n    \n    def _get_next_user_id(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Get next user ID.\"\"\"\n        schema_key = b\"_schema:_users\"\n        schema_data = self._system_db.get(schema_key)\n        if schema_data:\n            schema = json.loads(schema_data.decode())\n            next_id = str(schema[\"next_id\"])\n            schema[\"next_id\"] += 1\n            self._system_db.put(schema_key, json.dumps(schema).encode())\n            return next_id\n        return \"1\"\n    \n    def authenticate_user(self, username: str, password: str) -> tuple:\n        \"\"\"Authenticate user and return (success, is_admin, privileges).\"\"\"\n        prefix = b\"_users:\"\n        \n        for key, value in self._system_db.iterator(prefix=prefix):\n            user_data = json.loads(value.decode())\n            if user_data.get(\"username\") == username:\n                if self._verify_password(password, user_data.get(\"password_hash\", \"\")):\n                    is_admin = user_data.get(\"is_admin\", False)\n                    privileges = self._get_user_privileges(username)\n                    return (True, is_admin, privileges)\n                return (False, False, [])\n        \n        return (False, False, [])\n    \n    def _get_user_privileges(self, username: str) -> List[Dict]:\n        \"\"\"Get all privileges for a user.\"\"\"\n        privileges = []\n        prefix = b\"_privileges:\"\n        \n        for key, value in self._system_db.iterator(prefix=prefix):\n            priv_data = json.loads(value.decode())\n            if priv_data.get(\"username\") == username:\n                privileges.append({\n                    \"db\": priv_data.get(\"db_pattern\"),\n                    \"table\": priv_data.get(\"table_pattern\"),\n                    \"privs\": priv_data.get(\"privileges\", [])\n                })\n        \n        return privileges\n    \n    def grant_privilege(self, username: str, db_pattern: str, table_pattern: str, \n                      privileges: List[str]) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Grant privileges to a user.\"\"\"\n        self._ensure_system_tables()\n        \n        priv_id = self._get_next_privilege_id()\n        priv_data = {\n            \"id\": priv_id,\n            \"username\": username,\n            \"db_pattern\": db_pattern,\n            \"table_pattern\": table_pattern,\n            \"privileges\": privileges\n        }\n        \n        key = f\"_privileges:{priv_id}\".encode()\n        self._system_db.put(key, json.dumps(priv_data).encode())\n        return f\"Granted {','.join(privileges)} on {db_pattern}.{table_pattern} to '{username}'\"\n    \n    def _get_next_privilege_id(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Get next privilege ID.\"\"\"\n        schema_key = b\"_schema:_privileges\"\n        schema_data = self._system_db.get(schema_key)\n        if schema_data:\n            schema = json.loads(schema_data.decode())\n            next_id = str(schema[\"next_id\"])\n            schema[\"next_id\"] += 1\n priv in privileges:\n            # Check database pattern\n            db_match = priv[\"db\"] == \"*\" or priv[\"db\"] == db_name\n            \n            # Check table pattern\n            table_match = priv[\"table\"] == \"*\" or priv[\"table\"] == table_name\n            \n            # Check privilege\n            if db_match and table_match:\n                if \"ALL\" in {}\n        for col in columns:\n            widths[col] = len(col)\n        \n        for row in results:\n            for col in columns:\n                val_str = str(row.get(col, \"NULL\"))\n Create session\n        token = secrets.token_hex(16)\n        user_info = {\n            \"username\": username,\n            \"is_admin\": is_admin,\n            \"privileges\": privileges\n        }\n        self.active_sessions[token] = user_info\n        \n        return True, token, user_info\n    \n    def validate_session(self, token: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Check if session token is valid.\"\"\"\n        return token in self.active_sessions\n    \n    def get_user_info(self, token: str) -> Optional[Dict]:\n        \"\"\"Get user info from session token.\"\"\"\n        return self.active_sessions.get(token)\n    \n    def end_session(self, token: str):\n        \"\"\"End a session.\"\"\"\n        if token in self.active_sessions:\n            del self.active_sessions[token]\n    \n    def check_privilege(self, token: str, db_name: str, table_name: str, \n                       required_priv: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Check if user has required privilege.\"\"\"\n        user_info = self.get_user_info(token)\n        if not user_info:\n            return False\n        \n        username = user_info[\"username\"]\n        is_admin = user_info.get(\"is_admin\", False)\n        \n        # = parts[0].upper()\n        \n        if cmd == \"USER\":\n            if len(parts) < 2:\n                return \"ERROR: Username required\"\n            self.pending_username = parts[1].strip()\n
