<!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "<updateTask><id>1783140379.7139697</id><status>in_progress</status></updateTask>\n\nNow I'll implement Task 4 - the replication protocol. This involves creating a replication module where slaves connect to masters and stream binlog entries:\n\n<WriteFile><fileName>replication.py</fileName><contentOfFile>\"\"\"\nReplication Protocol for LevelDB Socket Server\n\nImplements master-slave and master-master replication over TCP sockets.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport socket\nimport threading\nimport json\nimport time\nfrom typing import Optional, Dict, Any, List\nfrom database import Database\n\n\nclass ReplicationClient(threading.Thread):\n    \"\"\"\n    Replication client that runs on slave servers.\n    Connects to master and streams binlog entries.\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, master_host: str, master_port: int, \n                 username: str, password: str,\n                 db: Database, server_id: int):\n        super().__init__(daemon=True)\n        self.master_host = master_host\n        self.master_port = master_port\n        self.username = username\n        self.password = password\n        self.db = db\n        self.server_id = server_id\n        \n        self.socket: Optional[socket.socket] = None\n        self.running = False\n        self.connected = False\n        self.last_position = 0\n        self.reconnect_delay = 5  # seconds\n        self.max_reconnect_delay = 60  # max backoff\n    \n    def load_position(self) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Load last applied position from disk.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            if self.db._system_db:\n                pos_data = self.db._system_db.get(b\"_replication:last_position\")\n                if pos_data:\n                    return int(pos_data.decode())\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"[REPLICATION] Error loading position: {e}\")\n        return 0\n    \n    def save_position(self, position: int):\n        \"\"\"Save last applied position to disk.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            if self.db._system_db:\n                self.db._system_db.put(\n                    b\"_replication:last_position\", \n                    str(position).encode()\n                )\n                self.last_position = position\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"[REPLICATION] Error saving position: {e}\")\n    \n    def connect(self) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Connect to master server.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            self.socket = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)\n            self.socket.settimeout(30)\n            self.socket.connect((self.master_host, self.master_port))\n            \n            # Authenticate as replication user\n            auth_msg = f\"REPL AUTH {self.username} {self.password}\\n\"\n            self.socket.sendall(auth_msg.encode())\n            \n            response = self.socket.recv(4096).decode().strip()\n            if not response.startswith(\"OK\"):\n                print(f\"[REPLICATION] Auth failed: {response}\")\n                return False\n            \n            # Request binlog stream from last position\n            self.last_position = self.load_position()\n            stream_msg = f\"REPL STREAM FROM {self.last_position}\\n\"\n            self.socket.sendall(stream_msg.encode())\n            \n            response = self.socket.recv(4096).decode().strip()\n            if not response.startswith(\"OK\"):\n                print(f\"[REPLICATION] Stream request failed: {response}\")\n                return False\n            \n            self.connected = True\n            self.reconnect_delay = 5  # Reset backoff\n            print(f\"[REPLICATION] Connected to master at {self.master_host}:{self.master_port}\")\n            print(f\"[REPLICATION] Starting from position {self.last_position}\")\n            return True\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"[REPLICATION] Connection failed: {e}\")\n            return False\n    \n    def disconnect(self):\n        \"\"\"Disconnect from master.\"\"\"\n        self.connected = False\n        if self.socket:\n            try:\n                self.socket.close()\n            except:\n                pass\n            self.socket = None\n    \n    def apply_entry(self, entry: Dict) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"\n        Apply a binlog entry to local database.\n        Skip entries from our own server_id (loop prevention).\n        \"\"\"\n        # Skip our own entries (for master-master)\n        if entry.get('server_id') == self.server_id:\n            return True\n        \n        try:\n            op = entry['operation']\n            db_name = entry['database']\n            table = entry.get('table')\n            data = entry.get('data', {})\n            \n            # Ensure we're using the correct database\n            if db_name and self.db.current_db != db_name:\n                self.db.use_database(db_name)\n            \n            # Apply based on operation type\n            if op == 'INSERT':\n                if table and 'row' in data:\n                    # Reconstruct values from row\n                    row = data['row']\n                    # Get schema to determine column order\n                    schema_key = f\"_schema:{table}\".encode()\n                    schema_data = self.db._db.get(schema_key)\n                    if schema_data:\n                        schema = json.loads(schema_data.decode())\n                        values = [row.get(col) for col in schema['columns']]\n                        self.db.insert(table, values)\n            \n            elif op == 'UPDATE':\n                if table and 'set_clause' in data:\n                    self.db.update(table, data['set_clause'], data.get('where'))\n            \n            elif op == 'DELETE':\n                if table:\n                    self.db.delete(table, data.get('where'))\n            \n            elif op == 'CREATE_DB':\n                if 'db_name' in data:\n                    self.db.create_database(data['db_name'])\n            \n            elif op == 'DROP_DB':\n                if 'db_name' in data:\n                    self.db.drop_database(data['db_name'])\n            \n            elif op == 'CREATE_TABLE':\n                if 'table_name' in data and 'columns' in data:\n                    self.db.create_table(data['table_name'], data['columns'])\n            \n            elif op == 'DROP_TABLE':\n                if 'table_name' in data:\n                    self.db.drop_table(data['table_name'])\n            \n            # Save position after successful apply\n            self.save_position(entry['position'])\n            return True\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"[REPLICATION] Error applying entry {entry.get('position')}: {e}\")\n            return False\n    \n    def run(self):\n        \"\"\"Main replication loop.\"\"\"\n        self.running = True\n        \n        while self.running:\n            if not self.connected:\n                if not self.connect():\n                    # Backoff and retry\n                    print(f\"[REPLICATION] Retrying in {self.reconnect_delay}s...\")\n                    time.sleep(self.reconnect_delay)\n                    self.reconnect_delay = min(self.reconnect_delay * 2, self.max_reconnect_delay)\n                    continue\n            \n            try:\n                # Read binlog entry from master\n                data = self.socket.recv(4096)\n                if not data:\n                    print(\"[REPLICATION] Connection closed by master\")\n                    self.disconnect()\n                    continue\n                \n                # Parse entry (may be multiple lines)\n                lines = data.decode().strip().split('\\n')\n                for line in lines:\n                    line = line.strip()\n                    if not line:\n                        continue\n                    \n                    if line.startswith(\"REPL ENTRY\"):\n                        # Parse: REPL ENTRY position timestamp server_id db table op {data}\n                        parts = line.split(' ', 7)\n                        if len(parts) >= 7:\n                            entry = {\n                                'position': int(parts[2]),\n                                'timestamp': float(parts[3]),\n                                'server_id': int(parts[4]),\n                                'database': parts[5],\n                                'operation': parts[6],\n                                'data': json.loads(parts[7]) if len(parts) > 7 else {}\n                            }\n                            \n                            if self.apply_entry(entry):\n                                print(f\"[REPLICATION] Applied entry {entry['position']}: {entry['operation']}\")\n                            else:\n                                print(f\"[REPLICATION] Failed to apply entry {entry['position']}\")\n                    \n                    elif line.startswith(\"REPL HEARTBEAT\"):\n                        # Heartbeat from master - update position\n                        parts = line.split()\n                        if len(parts) >= 3:\n                            pos = int(parts[2])\n                            self.save_position(pos)\n                    \n                    elif line.startswith(\"ERROR\"):\n                        print(f\"[REPLICATION] Master error: {line}\")\n                        self.disconnect()\n                        break\n            \n            except socket.timeout:\n                # Timeout is OK, just continue\n                pass\n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f\"[REPLICATION] Error in replication loop: {e}\")\n                self.disconnect()\n        \n        self.disconnect()\n        print(\"[REPLICATION] Client stopped\")\n    \n    def stop(self):\n        \"\"\"Stop the replication client.\"\"\"\n        self.running = False\n        self.disconnect()\n\n\nclass ReplicationHandler(threading.Thread):\n    \"\"\"\n    Handles replication connections on the master server.\n    Streams binlog entries to connected slaves.\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, client_socket: socket.socket, address: tuple,\n                 db: Database, authenticator):\n        super().__init__(daemon=True)\n        self.client_socket = client_socket\n        self.address = address\n        self.db = db\n        self.authenticator = authenticator\n        self.running = True\n        self.authenticated = False\n        self.username = None\n        self.start_position = 0\n    \n    def send(self, message: str):\n        \"\"\"Send message to slave.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            self.client_socket.sendall((message + '\\n').encode())\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"[REPLICATION] Send error to {self.address}: {e}\")\n            self.running = False\n    \n    def handle_auth(self, line: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Handle REPL AUTH command.\"\"\"\n        parts = line.split()\n        if len(parts) >= 4 and parts[0] == \"REPL\" and parts[1] == \"AUTH\":\n            username = parts[2]\n            password = parts[3]\n            \n            # Authenticate\n            success, token, user_info = self.authenticator.authenticate(username, password)\n            if success:\n                # Check if user has REPLICATION_SLAVE privilege\n                if self.authenticator.is_replication_user(token):\n                    self.authenticated = True\n                    self.username = username\n                    self.send(\"OK: Authentication successful\")\n                    return True\n            \n            self.send(\"ERROR: Authentication failed or insufficient privileges\")\n            return False\n        \n        self.send(\"ERROR: Expected REPL AUTH\")\n        return False\n    \n    def handle_stream_request(self, line: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Handle REPL STREAM FROM command.\"\"\"\n        parts = line.split()\n        if len(parts) >= 4 and parts[0] == \"REPL\" and parts[1] == \"STREAM\" and parts[2] == \"FROM\":\n            try:\n                self.start_position = int(parts[3])\n                self.send(f\"OK: Starting stream from position {self.start_position}\")\n                print(f\"[REPLICATION] Slave {self.address} ({self.username}) starting from position {self.start_position}\")\n                return True\n            except ValueError:\n                self.send(\"ERROR: Invalid position\")\n                return False\n        \n        self.send(\"ERROR: Expected REPL STREAM FROM\")\n        return False\n    \n    def stream_binlog(self):\n        \"\"\"Stream binlog entries to slave.\"\"\"\n        last_sent_position = self.start_position\n        \n        while self.running and self.authenticated:\n            try:\n                # Get entries from binlog\n                if self.db._binlog:\n                    entries = self.db._binlog.get_entries(last_sent_position, limit=100)\n                    \n                    if entries:\n                        for entry in entries:\n                            # Format: REPL ENTRY position timestamp server_id db op {data}\n                            data_json = json.dumps(entry.get('data', {}))\n                            msg = (f\"REPL ENTRY {entry['position']} {entry['timestamp']} \"\n                                   f\"{entry['server_id']} {entry['database']} \"\n                                   f\"{entry['operation']} {data_json}\")\n                            self.send(msg)\n                            last_sent_position = entry['position']\n                    else:\n                        # No new entries, send heartbeat\n                        current_pos = self.db._binlog.get_latest_position()\n                        if current_pos > last_sent_position:\n                            # There might be new entries, try again\n                            continue\n                        self.send(f\"REPL HEARTBEAT {current_pos}\")\n                \n                # Small delay to prevent busy-waiting\n                time.sleep(0.1)\n                \n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f\"[REPLICATION] Stream error for {self.address}: {e}\")\n                self.running = False\n                break\n    \n    def run(self):\n        \"\"\"Handle the replication connection.\"\"\"\n        print(f\"[REPLICATION] Slave connected from {self.address}\")\n        \n        try:\n            # Set timeout for initial handshake\n            self.client_socket.settimeout(60)\n            \n            # Wait for authentication\n            data = self.client_socket.recv(4096)\n            if not data:\n                return\n            \n            line = data.decode().strip()\n            if not self.handle_auth(line):\n                return\n            \n            # Wait for stream request\n            data = self.client_socket.recv(4096)\n            if not data:\n                return\n            \n            line = data.decode().strip()\n            if not self.handle_stream_request(line):\n                return\n            \n            # Start streaming\n            self.client_socket.settimeout(None)  # No timeout during streaming\n            self.stream_binlog()\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"[REPLICATION] Handler error for {self.address}: {e}\")\n        finally:\n            print(f\"[REPLICATION] Slave {self.address} disconnected\")\n            try:\n                self.client_socket.close()\n            except:\n                pass\n\n\nclass ReplicationServer(threading.Thread):\n    \"\"\"\n    Server that listens for replication connections on a separate port.\n    Runs on master servers.\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, host: str, port: int, db: Database, authenticator):\n        super().__init__(daemon=True)\n        self.host = host\n        self.port = port\n        self.db = db\n        self.authenticator = \"\"\"Start listening for replication connections.\"\"\"\n        self.server_socket = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)\n        self.server_socket.setsockopt(socket.SOL_SOCKET, socket.SO_REUSEADDR, 1)\n        self.server_socket.bind((self.host, self.port))\n        self.server_socket.listen(5)\n        self.running = True\n        \n        print(f\"[REPLICATION] Server listening on {self.host}:{self.port}\")\n        \n        try:\n            while self.running:\n                self.server_socket.settimeout(1.0)\n                try:\n                    client_socket, address = self.server_socket.accept()\n                    handler = ReplicationHandler(client_socket, address, self.db, self.authenticator)\n                    self.handlers.append(handler)\n                    handler.start()\n                except socket.timeout:\n                    continue\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"[REPLICATION] Server error: {e}\")\n        finally:\n            self.stop()\n    \n    def stop(self):\n        \"\"\"Stop the replication server.\"\"\"\n        self.running = False\n      if len(parts) < 2:\n                return \"ERROR: Username required\"\n            self.pending_username = parts[1].strip()\n            return \"OK: Send PASS <password>\"\n        \n <!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "\"\"\"\nSQL-like Command Parser for LevelDB Socket Server\n\"\"\"\n\nimport re\nfrom typing import Dict, Any, Optional, Tuple\n\n\nclass CommandParser:\n    \"\"\"Parse SQL-like commands for LevelDB operations\"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.patterns = {\n            'CREATE': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*CREATE\\s+TABLE\\s+(?P<table>\\w+)(?:\\s*\\((?P<columns>[^)]+)\\))?\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'DROP': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*DROP\\s+TABLE\\s+(?P<table>\\w+)\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'INSERT': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*INSERT\\s+INTO\\s+(?P<table>\\w+)\\s+VALUES\\s*\\((?P<values>[^)]+)\\)\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'SELECT': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*SELECT\\s+(?P<columns>[\\w\\s*,]+)\\s+FROM\\s+(?P<table>\\w+)'\n                r'(?:\\s+WHERE\\s+(?P<where>.+?))?'\n                r'(?:\\s+ORDER\\s+BY\\s+(?P<order_by>\\w+)(?:\\s+(?P<order_dir>ASC|DESC))?)?\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'UPDATE': re.compile(\n self.authenticated:\n                    response = self._handle_auth(data)\n                    self.send(response)\n                    if response.startswith(\"ERROR\") or response == \"BYE\":\n                        break\n                    continue\n                \n                cmd_type, params = self.parser.parse(data)\n                \n                # Check privileges\n                if not self._check_privileges(cmd_type, params):\n                    self.send(\"ERROR: Permission denied\")\n                    continue\n                \n                response =            return \"ERROR: Invalid input\"\n        \n        cmd = parts[0].upper()\n        \n        if cmd == \"USER\":\n            if len(parts) < 2:\n                return \"ERROR: Username required\"\n            self.pending_username = parts[1].strip()\n            return \"OK: Send PASS <password>\"\n        \n        elif cmd == \"PASS\":\n            if len(parts) < 2:\n                return \"ERROR: Password required\"\n            if not hasattr(self, 'pending_username'):\n                return \"ERROR: USER first\"\n            \n            password = parts[1].strip()\n            success, token, user_info = self.authenticator.authenticate(\n                self.pending_username, password\n            )\n            \n            if success:\n 'CREATE', 'DROP': 'DROP',\n            'INSERT': 'INSERT', 'SELECT': 'SELECT',\n            'UPDATE': 'UPDATE', 'DELETE': 'DELETE'\n        }\n        \n        if cmd_type in priv_map:\n self.replication_port = replication_port\n        self.peer_host = peer_host\n        \n        # Replication state\n        self.is_slave = (role == 'slave')\n        self.is_master_master = (peer_host is not None)\n        \n        self.db = Database(data_dir, server_id)\n        self.authenticator = Authenticator(self.db)\n        self.server_socket = None\n        self.running = False\n        \n        # Replication components (initialized later)\n        self.replication_server = None\n        self.replication_client = None\n    \n    def start(self):\n        # Start client socket server\n        self.server_socket = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)\n        self.server_socket.setsockopt(socket.SOL_SOCKET, socket.SO_REUSEADDR, 1)\n        self.server_socket.bind((self.host, self.port))\n        self.server_socket.listen(5)\n        self.running = True\n        \n        print(f\"[SERVER] Started on {self.host}:{self.port}\")\n        print(f\"[SERVER] Server ID: {self.server_id}\")\n        print(f\"[SERVER] Role: {self.role}\")\n        if self.is_slave and self.master_host:\n            print(f\"[SERVER] Master: {self.master_host}\")\n        if self.is_master_master:\n            print(f\"[SERVER] Peer: {self.peer_host}\")\n        print(f\"[SERVER] Data: {self.db.data_dir}\")\n        print(\"Press Ctrl+C to stop\")\n        \n        # Start replication components if configured\n        self._start_replication()\n        \n        try:\n            while self.running:\n                client_socket,          self.replication_client = ReplicationClient(\n                master_host=master_host,\n                master_port=master_port,\n                username=\"repl\",\n                password=\"repl\",\n                db=self.db,\n                server_id=self.server_id\n            )\n            self.replication_client.start()\n        \n        # Master-Master: Connect to peer\n        if self.peer_host:\n            print(f\"[REPLICATION] Master-Master mode - connecting to peer {self.peer_host}\")\n            parts = self.peer_host.split(':')\n            peer_host = parts[0]\n            peer_port = int(parts[1]) if len(parts) > 1 else 9999\n            \n            self.peer_replication_client = ReplicationClient(\n                master_host=peer_host,\n                master_port=peer_port,\n                username=\"repl\",\n                password=\"repl\",\n                db=self.db,\n    def stop(self):\n        self.running = False\n        if self.server_socket:\n            self.server_socket.close()\n        \n        # Stop replication components\n        if self.replication_client:\n            print(\"[REPLICATION] Stopping replication client...\")\n            self.replication_client.stop()\n        if hasattr(self, 'peer_replication_client') and self.peer_replication_client:\n            print(\"[REPLICATION] Stopping self.replication_server.stop()\n        \n        self.db.close()\n        print(\"[SERVER] Stopped\")\n    def stop(self):\n        self.running = False\n        if self.server_socket:\n            self.server_socket.close()\n        \n        # Stop replication components\n        if self.replication_client:\n            print(\"[REPLICATION] Stopping replication client...\")\n parser.add_argument('--host', default='0.0.0.0', help='Client host (default: 0.0.0.0)')\n    parser.add_argument('--port', type=int, default=9999, help='Client port (default: 9999)')\n    parser.add_argument('--data_dir', default='./data', help='Data directory (default: ./data)')\n    \n    # Replication options\n    parser.add_argument('--server-id', type=int, default=1, \n Wait for server to start\n        time.sleep(2)\n        \n        # Check if process is running\n        if self.slave_proc.poll() is not None:\n            self.log(\"ERROR: Slave failed to start\")\n            return False\n        \n        self.log(\"Slave started successfully\")\n        return True\n    \n    def stop_servers(self):\n        \"\"\"Stop all test servers.\"\"\"\n        self.log(\"Stopping servers...\")\n        \n        if self.slave_proc:\n            self.slave_proc.terminate()\n            self.slave_proc.wait()\n            self.slave_proc = None\n        \n        if self.master_proc:\n            self.master_proc.terminate()\n            self.master_proc.wait()\n            self.master_proc = None\n        \n        self.log(\"Servers stopped\")\n    \n    def send_command(self, host, port, commands):\n        \"\"\"Send commands to server and return responses.\"\"\"\n        responses = []\n        try:\n            sock = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)\n            sock.settimeout(10)\n            sock.connect((host, port))\n            \n            for cmd in commands:\n                sock.sendall((cmd + '\\n').encode())\n                time.sleep(0.5)\n                data = sock.recv(4096).decode()\n                responses.append(data)\n            \n            sock.close()\n        except Exception as e:\n            self.log(f\"Connection error: {e}\")\n            return None\n        \n        return responses\n    \n    def test_basic_replication(self):\n        \"\"\"Test basic master-slave replication.\"\"\"\n        self.log(\"=\" * 50)\n        self.log(\"TEST: Basic Replication\")\n        self.log(\"=\" * 50)\n        \n        try:\n            # Setup: Create replication user on master\n            self.log(\"Creating replication user...\")\n            \n            # Test 1: Connect to master and create database\n            self.log(\"Creating test database on master...\")\n            responses = self.send_command(\"localhost\", 9999, [\n                \"USER admin\",\n                \"PASS admin\",\n                \"CREATE DATABASE test_repl\",\n                \"USE test_repl\",\n                \"CREATE TABLE users (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name TEXT)\",\n                \"INSERT INTO users VALUES (1, 'Alice')\",\n                \"INSERT INTO users VALUES (2, 'Bob')\"\n            ])\n            \n            if not responses:\n                self.log(\"FAIL: Could not connect to master\")\n                return False\n            \n            self.log(\"Data inserted on master\")\n            \n            # Wait for replication\n            time.sleep(3)\n            \n            # Test 2: Check data on slave\n            self.log(\"Checking data on slave...\")\n            responses = self.send_command(\"localhost\", 9998, [\n                \"USER admin\",\n                \"PASS admin\",\n                \"USE test_repl\",\n                \"SELECT * FROM users\"\n            ])\n            \n            if not responses:\n                self.log(\"FAIL: Could not connect to slave\")\n                return False\n            \n            last_response = responses[-1] if responses else \"\"\n            if \"Alice\" in last_response and \"Bob\" in last_response:\n                self.log(\"PASS: Data replicated to slave\")\n                return True\n            else:\n                self.log(f\"FAIL: Data not found on slave. Response: {last_response}\")\n                return False\n                \n        except Exception as e:\n            self.log(f\"FAIL: Test error: {e}\")\n            return False\n    \n    def test_slave_recovery(self):\n        \"\"\"Test slave reconnection and catch-up.\"\"\"\n        self.log(\"=\" * 50)\n        self.log(\"TEST: Slave Recovery\")\n        self.log(\"=\" * 50)\n        \n        try:\n            # Stop slave\n            self.log(\"Stopping slave...\")\n            if self.slave_proc:\n                self.slave_proc.terminate()\n                self.slave_proc.wait()\n                self.slave_proc = None\n            \n            # Insert more data on master while slave is down\n            self.log(\"Inserting data while slave is down...\")\n            self.send_command(\"localhost\", 9999, [\n                \"USER admin\",\n                \"PASS admin\",\n                \"USE test_repl\",\n                \"INSERT INTO users VALUES (3, 'Charlie')\",\n                \"INSERT INTO users VALUES (4, 'David')\"\n            ])\n            \n            # Restart slave\n            self.log(\"Restarting slave...\")\n            if not self.start_slave():\n                self.log(\"FAIL: Could not restart slave\")\n                return False\n            \n            # Wait for catch-up\n            time.sleep(3)\n            \n            # Check all data is present\n            self.log(\"Verifying slave caught up...\")\n            responses = self.send_command(\"localhost\", 9998, [\n                \"USER admin\",\n                \"PASS admin\",\n                \"USE test_repl\",\n                \"SELECT * FROM users\"\n            ])\n            \n            if not responses:\n                self.log(\"FAIL: Could not connect to slave after restart\")\n                return False\n            \n            last_response = responses[-1] if responses else \"\"\n            if \"Charlie\" in last_response and \"David\" in last_response:\n                self.log(\"PASS: Slave recovered and caught up\")\n                return True\n            else:\n                self.log(f\"FAIL: Slave did not catch up. Response: {last_response}\")\n                return False\n                \n        except Exception as e:\n            self.log(f\"FAIL: Test error: {e}\")\n            return False\n    \n    def run_all_tests(self):\n        \"\"\"Run all replication tests.\"\"\"\n        self.log(\"Starting Replication Test Suite\")\n        self.log(\"=\" * 50)\n        \n        results = []\n        \n        try:\n            # Start master\n            if not self.start_master():\n                self.log(\"FAILED: Could not start master\")\n                return False\n            \n            # Create admin user on master first\n            time.sleep(1)\n            \n            # Start slave\n            if not self.start_slave():\n                self.log(\"FAILED: Could not start slave\")\n                self.stop_servers()\n                return False\n            \n            # Run tests\n            results.append((\"Basic Replication\", self.test_basic_replication()))\n            results.append((\"Slave Recovery\", self.test_slave_recovery()))\n            \n        finally:\n            # Cleanup\n            self.stop_servers()\n            self.cleanup_test_data()\n        \n        # Print summary\n        self.log(\"=\" * 50)\n        self.log(\"TEST SUMMARY\")\n        self.log(\"=\" * 50)\n        \n        passed = 0\n        failed = 0\n        \n        for name, result in results:\n            status = \"PASS\" if result else \"FAIL\"\n            self.log(f\"{name}: {status}\")\n            if result:\n                passed += 1\n            else:\n                failed += 1\n        \n        self.log(f\"\\nTotal: {passed} passed, {failed} failed\")\n        \n        return failed == 0\n    \n    def cleanup_test_data(self):\n        \"\"\"Remove test data directories.\"\"\"\n        import shutil\n        for data_dir in [\"./test_data_master\", \"./test_data_slave\"]:\n            if os.path.exists(data_dir):\n                try:\n                    shutil.rmtree(data_dir)\n                    self.log(f\"Cleaned up {data_dir}\")\n                except Exception as e:\n                    self.log(f\"Warning: Could not remove {data_dir}: {e}\")\n\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    test = ReplicationTest()\n    success = test.run_all_tests()\n    sys.exit(0 if success else 1)\n</contentOfFile></WriteFile>", "sessionId": 216, "rowId": 17, "timestamp": 1783140886.6864748, "date": "2026-07-04", "thinking": ""} -->

--data_dir ./data_master\n```\n\n**Step 2: Create Replication User**\n```bash\n# Connect to master\nnc localhost 9999\n> USER admin\n> PASS yourpassword\n> CREATE REPLICATION USER repl IDENTIFIED BY Start Server B**\n```bash\npython server.py --server-id 2 --port 9998 --replication-port 10998 --peer-host localhost:9999 --data_dir ./data_b\n```\n\n**Step 3: Test Bi-Directional INSERT INTO items VALUES (2, 'FromB')\n\n# Back to Server A, verify\n> SELECT * FROM items\n# Should see both: FromA, FromB\n```\n\n### Test 3: Replication Commands\n\n**SHOW MASTER STATUS**\n```sql\n> SHOW MASTER STATUS\n--------------------\nMaster Status\n--------------------\nBinlog Position: 150\nServer ID: 1\nConnected Slaves: 1\n--------------------\n```\n\n**SHOW SLAVE 150\nMaster Binlog Position: 150\n--------------------\n```\n\n**RESET SLAVE**\n```sql\n> RESET SLAVE\nOK: Slave reset - will start from beginning\n```\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Slave not connecting\n- Check firewall settings\n- Verify master is running with `--replication-port`\n- Check replication user exists with correct password\n\n### Data not replicating\n- Check `SHOW MASTER STATUS` on master\n- Check `SHOW SLAVE STATUS` on slave\n- Look for errors in server logs\n- Verify network connectivity\n\n### Conflict in Master-Master\n- Each server should have unique `--server-id`\n- The replication protocol skips entries from same server-id\n- Last-write-wins based on timestamp\n\n## Expected Behavior\n\n1. **Master-Slave**: All writes on master appear on slave within seconds\n2. **Slave Recovery**: When slave reconnects, it catches up on missed entries\n3. **Master-Master**: Writes on either server appear on the other\n4. **Loop Prevention**: Entries are not re-applied to originating server\n\n## Performance Notes\n\n- Replication is asynchronous (not waiting for slave acknowledgment)\n- Binlog entries are streamed in batches\n- Position tracking ensures no duplicate processing\n- Exponential backoff on connection failures\n</contentOfFile></WriteFile>", "sessionId": 216, "rowId": 17, "timestamp": 1783140897.8919463, "date": "2026-07-04", <!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "<updateTask><id>1783140379.7145884</id><status>completed</status></updateTask>\n<updateTask><id>1783140379.7147233</id><status>in_progress</status></updateTask>\n\nNow let me complete Task 10 - updating the README with replication documentation:\n\n<WriteFile><fileName>README.md</fileName><contentOfFile># LevelDB Socket Server\n\nA threaded Python socket server providing a MySQL-like command interface over LevelDB backend with database-backed authentication, privilege management, and replication.\n\n## Features\n\n- **Threaded TCP Socket Server** - Handles multiple concurrent clients\n- **Database-Backed Authentication** - User accounts stored in LevelDB with hashed passwords\n- **Privilege System** - Role-based access control (admin/users) with database/table-level permissions\n- **Admin User Management** - Create admin users via command line\n- **Binary Log (Binlog)** - All writes logged for replication\n- **Master-Slave Replication** - One master, multiple slaves\n- **Master-Master Replication** - Bi-directional replication between peers\n- **Automatic Recovery** - Slaves reconnect and catch up on missed data\n- **LevelDB Backend** - Persistent key-value storage with table namespacing\n- **SQL-like Commands** - CREATE, DROP, INSERT, SELECT, UPDATE, DELETE\n- **Advanced Querying** - WHERE clauses, ORDER BY sorting, indexed columns\n- **Netcat Compatible** - Test with standard netcat client\n\n## Installation\n\n```bash\npip install -r requirements.txt\n```\n\n## Quick Start\n\n### 1. Create an Admin User\n\nBefore first use, create an admin user:\n\n```bash\npython server.py --prepare_admin admin --prepare_password yourpassword\n```\n\nOr interactively (password will be prompted):\n\n```bash\npython server.py --prepare_admin admin\n```\n\n### 2. Start the Server\n\n```bash\npython server.py\n```\n\nServer will start on port 9999 with default settings.\n\nOptions:\n```bash\npython server.py --host 0.0.0.0 --port 9999 --data_dir ./data\n```\n\n### 3. Connect with Netcat\n\n```bash\nnc localhost 9999\n```\n\n## Replication Setup\n\n### Master-Slave Replication\n\n**Start Master:**\n```bash\npython server.py --server-id 1 --role master --replication-port 10999 --data_dir ./data_master\n```\n\n**Create Replication User on Master:**\n```sql\nCREATE REPLICATION USER 'repl' IDENTIFIED BY 'replpass';\n```\n\n**Start Slave:**\n```bash\npython server.py --server-id 2 --role slave --master-host localhost:9999 --data_dir ./data_slave\n```\n\n### Master-Master Replication\n\n**Server A:**\n```bash\npython server.py --server-id 1 --port 9999 --replication-port 10999 --peer-host localhost:9998 --data_dir ./data_a\n```\n\n**Server B:**\n```bash\npython server.py --server-id 2 --port 9998 --replication-port 10998 --peer-host localhost:9999 --data_dir ./data_b\n```\n\n## Authentication\n\nThe server requires authentication before accepting <password>\n--------------------------------------------------\n\nUSER admin\nOK: Send PASS <password>\n\nPASS yourpassword\nOK: Welcome admin (admin).\n```\n\n## Available Commands\n\n### Database TABLE <name> (col1 [PRIMARY KEY], col2 [INDEX], ...)` | Create table with optional indexes |\n| `DROP TABLE <name>` | Delete a table |\n\n### Data Commands\n| Command | Description |\n|---------|-------------|\n| `INSERT INTO <table> VALUES (val1, val2, ...)` | Insert a record |\n| `SELECT * FROM <table>` | Select all records |\n| `SELECT * FROM <table> ORDER BY col # LevelDB Socket Server
> 
> A threaded Python socket server providing a MySQL-like command interface over LevelDB backend with database-backed authentication, privilege management, and replication.
> 
> ## Features
> 
> - **Threaded TCP Socket Server** - Handles multiple concurrent clients
> - **Database-Backed Authentication** - User accounts stored in LevelDB with hashed passwords
> - **Privilege System** - Role-based access control (admin/users) with database/table-level permissions
> - **Admin User Managemen...
> (truncated, 9426 chars total)

---

<!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "# LevelDB Socket Server\n\nA threaded Python socket server providing a MySQL-like command interface over LevelDB backend with database-backed authentication, privilege management, and replication.\n\n## Features\n\n- **Threaded TCP Socket Server** - Handles multiple concurrent clients\n- **Database-Backed Authentication** - User accounts stored in LevelDB with hashed passwords\n- **Privilege System** - Role-based access control (admin/users) with database/table-level permissions\n- **Admin User Management** - Create admin users via command line\n- **Binary Log (Binlog)** - All writes logged for replication\n- **Master-Slave Replication** - One master, multiple slaves\n- **Master-Master Replication** - Bi-directional replication between peers\n- **Automatic Recovery** - Slaves reconnect and catch up on missed data\n- **LevelDB Backend** - Persistent key-value storage with table namespacing\n- **SQL-like Commands** - CREATE, DROP, INSERT, SELECT, UPDATE, DELETE\n- **Advanced Querying** - WHERE clauses, ORDER BY sorting, indexed columns\n- **Netcat Compatible** - Test with standard netcat client\n\n## Installation\n\n```bash\npip install -r requirements.txt\n```\n\n## Quick Start\n\n### 1. Create an Admin User\n\nBefore first use, create an admin user:\n\n```bash\npython server.py --prepare_admin admin --prepare_password yourpassword\n```\n\nOr interactively (password will be prompted):\n\n```bash\npython server.py --prepare_admin admin\n```\n\n### 2. Start the Server\n\n```bash\npython server.py\n```\n\nServer will start on port 9999 with default settings.\n\nOptions:\n```bash\npython server.py --host 0.0.0.0 --port 9999 --data_dir ./data\n```\n\n### 3. Connect with Netcat\n\n```bash\nnc localhost 9999\n```\n\n## Replication Setup\n\n### Master-Slave Replication\n\n**Start Master:**\n```bash\npython server.py --server-id 1 --role master --replication-port 10999 --data_dir ./data_master\n```\n\n**Create Replication User on Master:**\n```sql\nCREATE REPLICATION USER 'repl' IDENTIFIED BY 'replpass';\n```\n\n**Start Slave:**\n```bash\npython server.py --server-id 2 --role slave --master-host localhost:9999 --data_dir ./data_slave\n```\n\n### Master-Master Replication\n\n**Server A:**\n```bash\npython server.py --server-id 1 --port 9999 --replication-port 10999 --peer-host localhost:9998 --data_dir ./data_a\n```\n\n**Server B:**\n```bash\npython server.py --server-id 2 --port 9998 --replication-port 10998 --peer-host localhost:9999 --data_dir ./data_b\n```\n\n## Authentication\n\nThe server requires authentication before accepting commands:\n\n```\n==================================================\nLevelDB Socket Server\n==================================================\nAuthentication required\nUSER <username> then PASS <password>\n--------------------------------------------------\n\nUSER admin\nOK: Send PASS <password>\n\nPASS yourpassword\nOK: Welcome admin (admin).\n```\n\n## Available Commands\n\n### Database Commands\n| Command | Description |\n|---------|-------------|\n| `SHOW DATABASES` | List all databases |\n| `CREATE DATABASE <name>` | Create a new database |\n| `DROP DATABASE <name>` | Delete a database |\n| `USE <database>` | Select database to use |\n\n### Table Commands\n| Command | Description |\n|---------|-------------|\n| `SHOW TABLES` | List tables in current database |\n| `CREATE TABLE <name> (col1 [PRIMARY KEY], col2 [INDEX], ...)` | Create table with optional indexes |\n| `DROP TABLE <name>` | Delete a table |\n\n### Data Commands\n| Command | Description |\n|---------|-------------|\n| `INSERT INTO <table> VALUES (val1, val2, ...)` | Insert a record |\n| `SELECT * FROM <table>` | Select all records |\n| `SELECT * FROM <table> ORDER BY col [ASC\\|DESC]` | Select with sorting |\n| `SELECT col FROM <table> WHERE condition` | Select with filter |\n| `UPDATE <table> SET col=val WHERE condition` | Update records |\n| `DELETE FROM <table> WHERE condition` | Delete records |\n\n### Replication Commands (Admin Only)\n| Command | Description |\n|---------|-------------|\n| `SHOW MASTER STATUS` | Show binlog position and connected slaves |\n| `SHOW SLAVE STATUS` | Show replication status and lag |\n| `START SLAVE` | Start replication |\n| `STOP SLAVE` | Stop replication |\n| `RESET SLAVE` | Reset replication position |\n| `CREATE REPLICATION USER <name> IDENTIFIED BY <pass>` | Create replication user |\n\n### Admin Commands\n| Command | Description |\n|---------|-------------|\n| `SHOW USERS` | List all users |\n| `HELP` | Show available commands |\n| `QUIT` / `EXIT` | Disconnect |\n\n## Example Session\n\n### Basic Operations\n```\n> CREATE DATABASE testdb\nOK: Database 'testdb' created\n\n> USE testdb\nOK: Switched to database 'testdb'\n\n> CREATE TABLE users (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name TEXT, email TEXT INDEX)\nOK: Table 'users' created\n\n> INSERT INTO users VALUES (1, 'John', 'john@example.com')\nOK: Inserted 1 row into 'users'\n\n> INSERT INTO users VALUES (2, 'Jane', 'jane@example.com')\nOK: Inserted 1 row into 'users'\n\n> SELECT * FROM users\n+----+-------+------------------+\n| id | name  | email            |\n+----+-------+------------------+\n| 1  | John  | john@example.com |\n| 2  | Jane  | jane@example.com |\n+----+-------+------------------+\n2 row(s) in set\n\n> SELECT * FROM users ORDER BY name DESC\n+----+-------+------------------+\n| id | name  | email            |\n+----+-------+------------------+\n| 2  | Jane  | jane@example.com |\n| 1  | John  | john@example.com |\n+----+-------+------------------+\n1 row(s) in set\n\n> UPDATE users SET name='Johnny' WHERE id=1\nOK: Updated 1 row(s) in 'users'\n\n> DELETE FROM users WHERE id=2\nOK: Deleted 1 row(s) from 'users'\n\n> DROP TABLE users\nOK: Table 'users' dropped\n\n> DROP DATABASE testdb\nOK: Database 'testdb' dropped\n```\n\n### Replication Commands\n```\n> SHOW MASTER STATUS\n--------------------------------------------------\nMaster Status\n--------------------------------------------------\nBinlog Position: 150\nServer ID: 1\nConnected Slaves: 1\n--------------------------------------------------\n\n> SHOW SLAVE STATUS\n--------------------------------------------------\nSlave Status\n--------------------------------------------------\nSlave IO State: Connected\nMaster Host: localhost\nMaster Port: 9999\nLast Applied Position: 150\nMaster Binlog Position: 150\n--------------------------------------------------\n```\n\n## Table Schema Options\n\nWhen creating tables, you can specify indexes:\n\n```sql\nCREATE TABLE products (\n    id INT PRIMARY KEY,        -- Primary key for fast lookup\n    name TEXT,                 -- Regular column\n    category TEXT INDEX,       -- Indexed for fast filtering\n    price FLOAT INDEX          -- Indexed for sorting\n)\n```\n\n## Command-Line Options\n\n```\nusage: server.py [-h] [--prepare_admin USER] [--prepare_password PASS]\n                 [--host HOST] [--port PORT] [--data_dir DATA_DIR]\n                 [--server-id SERVER_ID] [--role {master,slave}]\n                 [--master-host HOST:PORT] [--replication-port PORT]\n                 [--peer-host HOST:PORT]\n\nLevelDB Socket Server with Replication\n\noptional arguments:\n  -h, --help            show this help message and exit\n  --prepare_admin USER  Create admin user\n  --prepare_password PASS\n                        Admin password\n  --host HOST           Client host (default: 0.0.0.0)\n  --port PORT           Client port (default: 9999)\n  --data_dir DATA_DIR   Data directory (default: ./data)\n  --server-id SERVER_ID\n                        Unique server ID (default: 1)\n  --role {master,slave}\n                        Server role: master or slave (default: master)\n  --master-host HOST:PORT\n                        Master host:port for slave replication\n  --replication-port PORT\n                        Port for replication connections (optional)\n  --peer-host HOST:PORT\n                        Peer host:port for master-master replication\n```\n\n## Project Structure\n\n```\nt10/\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 server.py              # Main server entry point\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 database.py            # LevelDB wrapper with binlog integration\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 auth.py               # Session-based authentication\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 binlog.py             # Binary log for replication\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 replication.py        # Replication client/server\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 replication_commands.py  # Replication control commands\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 parser.py             # SQL command parser\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 commands.py           # Command execution framework\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 tests/\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 test_client.py    # Basic client tests\n\u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 test_replication.py  # Replication tests\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 TESTING.md           # Testing documentation\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 requirements.txt      # Dependencies\n\u2514\u2500\u2500 README.md            # Documentation\n```\n\n## Configuration\n\nDefault settings:\n- **Host**: 0.0.0.0\n- **Port**: 9999\n- **Data Directory**: ./data\n- **System Database**: ./_system (stores users and privileges)\n- **Binlog**: ./_binlog (replication log)\n\n## Replication Architecture\n\n### Master-Slave\n```\n[Master] <--writes-- [Client]\n    |\n    | binlog stream\n    v\n[Slave] <--reads-- [Client]\n```\n\n### Master-Master\n```\n[Server A] <----> [Server B]\n   ^                   ^\n   |                   |\nwrites              writes\n```\n\n## Security Notes\n\n- Passwords are hashed with SHA-256 and a unique salt per user\n- Session tokens are generated using `secrets.token_hex()`\n- Privileges are checked for every database operation\n- Admin users have full access to all databases and tables\n- Replication users can only stream binlog (no query access)\n\n## Testing\n\nRun automated tests:\n```bash\npython tests/test_client.py\npython tests/test_replication.py\n```\n\nSee [TESTING.md](TESTING.md) for detailed testing procedures.\n\n## License\n\nMIT", "sessionId": 216, "rowId": 19, "timestamp": > ## PHP Access

<!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "Great question! Here are the best approaches for both languages:\n\n## PHP Access\n\nSince our server uses a simple TCP socket protocol, PHP can connect directly using sockets:\n\n### Option 1: Native PHP Sockets (Recommended)\n\n```php\n<?php\nclass LevelDBClient {\n    private $socket;\n    private $host;\n    private $port;\n    \n    public function __construct($host = 'localhost', $port = 9999) {\n        $this->host = $host;\n        $this->port = $port;\n    }\n    \n    public function connect() {\n        $this->socket = fsockopen($this->host, $this->port, $errno, $errstr, 30);\n        if (!$this->socket) {\n            throw new Exception(\"Connection failed: $errstr ($errno)\");\n        }\n        // Read welcome message\n        $this->readLines(6);\n        return true;\n    }\n    \n    public function authenticate($username, $password) {\n        $this->send(\"USER $username\");\n        $response = $this->readLine();\n        if (!str_contains($response, 'OK')) return false;\n        \n        $this->send(\"PASS $password\");\n        $response = $this->readLine();\n        return str_contains($response, 'OK');\n    }\n    \n    public function query($sql) {\n        $this->send($sql);\n        return $this->readResponse();\n    }\n    \n    private function send($cmd) {\n        fwrite($this->socket, $cmd . \"\\n\");\n    }\n    \n    private function readLine() {\n        return trim(fgets($this->socket, 4096));\n    }\n    \n    private function readLines($count) {\n        $lines = [];\n        for ($i = 0; $i < $count; $i++) {\n            $lines[] = $this->readLine();\n        }\n        return $lines;\n    }\n    \n    private function readResponse() {\n        $response = '';\n        while ($line = $this->readLine()) {\n            if ($line === '') continue;\n            $response .= $line . \"\\n\";\n            // Check for end markers\n            if (str_starts_with($line, 'OK:') || \n                str_starts_with($line, 'ERROR:') ||\n                str_contains($line, 'row(s) in set')) {\n                break;\n            }\n        }\n        return $response;\n    }\n    \n    public function close() {\n        if ($this->socket) {\n            $this->send(\"QUIT\");\n            fclose($this->socket);\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// Usage\ntry {\n    $client = new LevelDBClient('localhost', 9999);\n    $client->connect();\n    \n    if ($client->authenticate('admin', 'admin')) {\n        echo \"Connected!\\n\";\n        \n        // Create database\n        echo $client->query(\"CREATE DATABASE myapp\");\n        \n        // Use database\n        echo $client->query(\"USE myapp\");\n        \n        // Create table\n        echo $client->query(\"CREATE TABLE users (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name TEXT, email TEXT)\");\n        \n        // Insert\n        echo $client->query(\"INSERT INTO users VALUES (1, 'John', 'john@example.com')\");\n        \n        // Select\n        $result = $client->query(\"SELECT * FROM users\");\n        echo $result;\n    }\n    \n    $client->close();\n} catch (Exception $e) {\n    echo \"Error: \" . $e->getMessage();\n}\n?>\n```\n\n### Option 2: PDO-Style Wrapper (More familiar API)\n\n```php\n<?php\nclass LevelDBPDO {\n    private $client;\n    \n    public function __construct($dsn) {\n        // Parse DSN like: leveldb:host=localhost;port=9999;dbname=mydb\n        parse_str(str_replace(';', '&', parse_url($dsn)['query'] ?? # Select\n        result = client.select('users')\n        print(result)\n        \n        # Or with WHERE\n        result = client.execute(\"SELECT * FROM users WHERE id=1\")\n leveldb_connection(host='localhost', port=9999, user='admin', password='admin'):\n    \"\"\"Context manager for database connections\"\"\"\n    client = LevelDBClient(host, port)\n    try:\n        client.connect()\n        if not client.auth(user, password):\n            raise Exception(\"Authentication failed\")\n        yield client\n    finally:\n        client.close()\n\n# Usage\nwith self.reader.readline()\n        \n        self.writer.write(f\"PASS {password}\\n\".encode())\n        await self.writer.drain()\n        response = await self.reader.readline()\n        return \"ERROR:\")):\n                break\n        return \"\\n\".join(response)\n    \n    async def close(self):\n        if self.writer:\n            self.writer.write(b\"QUIT\\n\")\n            await <!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "I'll create the example directories and files. client for connecting to the LevelDB Socket Server.\n * Supports authentication, queries, and result parsing.\n * \n * @author LevelDB Team\n * @version 1.0.0\n */\n\nclass LevelDBClient {\n    private $socket;\n    private $host;\n    private $port;\n    private $connected = false;\n    private $authenticated = false;\n    \n    /**\n     * Constructor\n     * \n     * @param string $host Server hostname (default: localhost)\n     * @param int $port Server port (default: 9999)\n     */\n    public function __construct($host = 'localhost', $port = 9999) {\n        $this->host = $host;\n        $this->port = $port;\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Connect to the LevelDB server\n     * \n     * @return bool True on success\n     * @throws Exception on connection failure\n     */\n    public function connect() {\n        $this->socket = @fsockopen($this->host, $this->port, $errno, $errstr, 30);\n        \n        if (!$this->socket) {\n            throw new Exception(\"Connection failed: $errstr ($errno)\");\n        }\n        \n        // Read welcome banner (6 lines)\n        $this->readLines(6);\n        \n        $this->connected = true;\n        return true;\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Authenticate with username and password\n     * \n     * @param string $username\n     * @param string $password\n     * @return bool True on successful authentication\n     * @throws Exception on auth failure\n     */\n    public function authenticate($username, $password) {\n        if (!$this->connected) {\n            throw new Exception(\"Not connected\");\n        }\n        \n        // Send USER command\n        $this->send(\"USER $username\");\n        $response = $this->readLine();\n        \n        if (strpos($response, 'OK') === false) {\n            throw new Exception(\"USER command failed: $response\");\n        }\n        \n        // Send PASS command\n        $this->send(\"PASS $password\");\n        $response = $this->readLine();\n        \n        if (strpos($response, 'OK') === false) {\n            throw new Exception(\"Authentication failed: $response\");\n        }\n        \n        $this->authenticated = true;\n        return true;\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Execute a SQL-like command\n     * \n     * @param string $sql The command to execute\n     * @return string Raw response from server\n     */\n    public function execute($sql) {\n        if (!$this->authenticated) {\n            throw new Exception(\"Not authenticated\");\n        }\n        \n        $this->send($sql);\n        return $this->readResponse();\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Execute a SELECT query and return parsed results\n     * \n     * @param string $sql SELECT query\n     * @return array Array of associative arrays representing rows\n     */\n    public function query($sql) {\n        $result = $this->execute($sql);\n        return $this->parseSelectResult($result);\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Create a database\n     * \n     *   \n    /**\n     * Drop a database\n     * \n     * @param string $name Database name\n     * @return string Response from server\n     */\n    public function dropDatabase($name) {\n        return $this->execute(\"DROP DATABASE $name\");\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Select database to use\n     * \n     * @param string $name Database name\n     * @return string Response from server\n     */\n    public function useDatabase($name) {\n        return $this->execute(\"USE $name\");\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Create a table\n     * \n     * @param string $name Table name\n     * @param array $columns Column definitions (e.g., ['id INT PRIMARY KEY', 'name TEXT'])\n     * @return string Response from server\n     */\n    public function createTable($name, array $columns) {\n        $cols = implode(', ', $columns);\n        return $this->execute(\"CREATE TABLE $name ($cols)\");\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Drop a table\n     * \n     * @param string $name Table name\n     * @return string Response from server\n     */\n    public function dropTable($name) {\n        return $this->execute(\"DROP TABLE $name\");\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Insert data into table\n     * \n     * @param string $table Table name\n     * @param array $values Values to insert\n     * @return string Response from server\n     */\n    public function insert($table, array $values) {\n        $vals = [];\n        foreach ($values as $v) {\n            if (is_string($v)) {\n                $vals[] = \"'\" . addslashes($v) . \"'\";\n            } else {\n                $vals[] = $v;\n            }\n        }\n        $valStr = implode(', ', $vals);\n        return $this->execute(\"INSERT INTO $table VALUES ($valStr)\");\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Select from table\n     * \n     * @param string $table Table name\n     * @param string|null $where Optional WHERE clause\n     * @param string|null $orderBy Optional ORDER BY column\n     * @param bool $desc Sort descending (default: false)\n     * @return array Parsed results\n     */\n    public function select($table, $where = null, $orderBy = null, $desc = false) {\n        $sql = \"SELECT * FROM $table\";\n        \n        if ($where) {\n            $sql .= \" WHERE $where\";\n        }\n        \n        if ($orderBy) {\n            $sql .= \" ORDER BY $orderBy\";\n            if ($desc) {\n                $sql .= \" DESC\";\n            }\n        }\n        \n        return $this->query($sql);\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Update rows\n     * \n     * @param string $table Table name\n     * @param string $set SET clause (e.g., \"name='New'\")\n     * @param string|null $where Optional WHERE clause\n     * @return string Response from server\n     */\n    public function update($table, $set, $where = null) {\n        $sql = \"UPDATE $table SET $set\";\n        if ($where) {\n            $sql .= \" WHERE $where\";\n        }\n        return $this->execute($sql);\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Delete rows\n     * \n     * @param string $table Table name\n     * @param string|null $where Optional WHERE clause\n     * @return string Response from server\n     */\n    public function delete($table, $where = null) {\n        $sql = \"DELETE FROM $table\";\n        if ($where) {\n            $sql .= \" WHERE $where\";\n        }\n        return $this->execute($sql);\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Show master status (replication)\n     * \n     * @return string Response from server\n     */\n    public function showMasterStatus() {\n        return $this->execute(\"SHOW MASTER STATUS\");\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Show slave status (replication)\n     * \n     * @return string Response from server\n     */\n    public function showSlaveStatus() {\n        return $this->execute(\"SHOW SLAVE STATUS\");\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * List databases\n     * \n     * @return array List of database names\n     */\n    public function listDatabases() {\n        $result = $this->execute(\"SHOW DATABASES\");\n        // Parse result\n        preg_match_all('/OK:\\s*\\n?((?:.|\\n)*)/', $result, $matches);\n        if (isset($matches[1][0])) {\n            return array_filter(explode(\"\\n\", trim($matches[1][0])));\n        }\n        return [];\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * List tables in current database\n     * \n     * @return array List of table names\n     */\n    public function listTables() {\n        $result = $this->execute(\"SHOW TABLES\");\n        preg_match_all('/OK:\\s*\\n?((?:.|\\n)*)/', $result, $matches);\n        if (isset($matches[1][0])) {\n            return array_filter(explode(\"\\n\", trim($matches[1][0])));\n        }\n        return [];\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Close connection\n     */\n    public function close() {\n        if ($this->socket) {\n            $this->send(\"QUIT\");\n            fclose($this->socket);\n            $this->socket = null;\n            $this->connected = false;\n            $this->authenticated = false;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Check if connected\n     * \n     * @return bool\n     */\n    public function isConnected() {\n        return $this->connected;\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Check if authenticated\n     * \n     * @return bool\n     */\n    public function isAuthenticated() {\n        return $this->authenticated;\n    }\n    \n    // Private helper methods\n    \n    private function send($cmd) {\n        fwrite($this->socket, $cmd . \"\\n\");\n    }\n    \n    private function readLine() {\n        return trim(fgets($this->socket, 4096));\n    }\n    \n    private function readLines($count) {\n        $lines = [];\n        for ($i = 0; $i < $count; $i++) {\n            $lines[] = $this->readLine();\n        }\n        return $lines;\n    }\n    \n    private function readResponse() {\n        $response = '';\n        $startTime = time();\n        \n        while (true) {\n            // Timeout strpos($line, '+-') === 0) {\n                continue;\n            }\n            \n            // Parse header row\n            if (strpos($line, '| id') !== false && empty($headers)) {\n                preg_match_all('/\\|\\s*(\\w+)\\s*/', $line, $matches);\n                $headers = array_filter($matches[1]);\n                $inTable = true;\n                continue;\n            }\n array_map('trim', array_slice($matches[1], 1));\n                \n                if (count($values) >= count($headers)) {\n                    $row = [];\n                    foreach ($headers as $i => $header) {\n                        $row[$header] = $values[$i] ?? null;\n                    }\n                    $rows[] = $row;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        \n        return $rows;\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Destructor - ensure connection is closed\n     */\n    public function __destruct() {\n        $this->close();\n    }\n}\n</contentOfFile></WriteFile>", <!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "<WriteFile><fileName>examples/python/leveldb_client.py</fileName><contentOfFile>#!/usr/bin/env python3\n\"\"\"\nLevelDB Socket Server - Python Client Library\n\nA comprehensive Python client for connecting to the LevelDB Socket Server.\nSupports synchronous and asynchronous operations, connection pooling,\nand result parsing.\n\nAuthor: LevelDB \"\"\"\n    Synchronous client for LevelDB Socket Server.\n    \n    Example:\n        client = LevelDBClient('localhost', 9999)\n        client.connect()\n        client.auth('admin', 'admin')\n        client.create_database('myapp')\n        client.use('myapp')\n        result = client.query(\"SELECT * FROM users\")\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, host: str = 'localhost', port: int = 9999, \n                 timeout: int = 30, encoding: str = 'utf-8'):\n        \"\"\"\n        Initialize client.\n        \n        Args:\n            host: Server hostname\n            port: Server port\n            timeout: Connection timeout in seconds\n            encoding: Character encoding\n        \"\"\"\n        self.host = host\n        self.port = port\n        self.timeout = timeout\n        self.encoding = encoding\n        self.socket: Optional[socket.socket] = None\n        self._connected = False\n        self._authenticated = False\n        self._current_db: Optional[str] = None\n    \n    def connect(self) -> 'LevelDBClient':\n        \"\"\"\n        Connect to the server.\n        \n        Returns:\n            self for method chaining\n            \n        Raises:\n            ConnectionError: If connection fails\n        \"\"\"\n        try:\n            self.socket = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)\n            self.socket.settimeout(self.timeout)\n            self.socket.connect((self.host, self.port))\n            \n            # Read welcome banner\n            self._read_lines(6)\n            \n            self._connected = True\n            return self\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            raise ConnectionError(f\"Failed to connect: {e}\")\n    \n    def auth(self, username: str, password: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"\n        Authenticate with the server.\n        \n        Args:\n            username: Username\n            password: Password\n            \n        Returns:\n            True if authentication successful\n            \n        Raises:\n            AuthenticationError: If authentication fails\n        \"\"\"\n        if not self._connected:\n            raise ConnectionError(\"Not connected\")\n        \n        # Send USER command\n        self._send(f\"USER {username}\")\n        response = self._read_line()\n        \n        if not response.startswith(\"OK\"):\n            raise AuthenticationError(f\"USER command failed: {response}\")\n        \n        # Send PASS command\n        self._send(f\"PASS {password}\")\n        response = self._read_line()\n        \n        if not response.startswith(\"OK\"):\n            raise AuthenticationError(f\"Authentication failed: {response}\")\n        \n        self._authenticated = True\n        return True\n    \n    def execute(self, sql: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"\n        Execute a SQL-like command.\n        \n        Args:\n            sql: Command to execute\n            \n        Returns:\n            Raw response string\n            \n        Raises:\n            ConnectionError: If not authenticated\n        \"\"\"\n        if not self._authenticated:\n            raise ConnectionError(\"Not authenticated\")\n        \n        self._send(sql)\n        return self._read_response()\n    \n    def query(self, sql: str) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Execute a SELECT query and return parsed results.\n        \n        Args:\n            sql: SELECT query\n            \n        Returns:\n            List of dictionaries representing rows\n        \"\"\"\n        result = self.execute(sql)\n        return self._parse_select_result(result)\n    \n    # Convenience methods\n    \n    def create_database(self, name: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Create a database.\"\"\"\n        return self.execute(f\"CREATE DATABASE {name}\")\n    \n    def drop_database(self, name: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Drop a database.\"\"\"\n        result = self.execute(f\"DROP DATABASE {name}\")\n        if self._current_db == name:\n            self._current_db = None\n        return result\n    \n    def definitions\n        \"\"\"\n        cols = \", \".join(columns)\n        return self.execute(f\"CREATE TABLE {name} ({cols})\")\n    \n    def drop_table(self, name: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Drop a table.\"\"\"\n        return self.execute(f\"DROP TABLE {name}\")\n    \n    def insert(self, table: str, values: List[Any]) -> str:\n        \"\"\"\n        Insert values into table.\n        \n        Args:\n            table: Table name\n            values: List of values\n        \"\"\"\n        vals = []\n        for v in values:\n            if isinstance(v, str):\n                vals.append(f\"'{v}'\")\n            else:\n                vals.append(str(v))\n        val_str = \", \".join(vals)\n        return self.execute(f\"INSERT INTO {table} VALUES ({val_str})\")\n    \n    def select(self, table: str, where: Optional[str] = None,\n               columns: Optional[List[str]] = None,\n               order_by: Optional[str] = None,\n               desc: bool = False) -> column list (default: all)\n            order_by: Optional ORDER BY column\n            desc: Sort descending\n            \n        Returns:\n            List of row dictionaries\n        \"\"\"\n        cols = \", \".join(columns) if columns else \"*\"\n        sql = f\"SELECT {cols} FROM {table}\"\n        \n        if where:\n            sql += f\" WHERE {where}\"\n        \n        if set_clause: str, where: Optional[str] = None) -> str:\n        \"\"\"\n        Update rows.\n        \n        Args:\n            table: Table name\n            set_clause: SET clause (e.g., \"name='New'\")\n            where: Optional WHERE clause\n        \"\"\"\n        sql = f\"UPDATE {table} SET {set_clause}\"\n        if where:\n            sql += f\" WHERE {where}\"\n        return self.execute(sql)\n    \n    def delete(self, table: str, where: Optional[str] = None) -> str:\n        \"\"\"\n        Delete rows.\n        \n        Args:\n            table: Table name\n            where: Optional WHERE clause\n        \"\"\"\n        sql = f\"DELETE FROM {table}\"\n        if where:\n            sql += f\" WHERE {where}\"\n        return self.execute(sql)\n    \n    def list_tables(self) -> List[str]:\n        \"\"\"List tables in current database.\"\"\"\n        result = self.execute(\"SHOW TABLES\")\n        return self._parse_list_result(result)\n    \n    def show_master_status(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Show replication master status.\"\"\"\n        return self.execute(\"SHOW MASTER STATUS\")\n    \n    def show_slave_status(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Show replication slave status.\"\"\"\n        return self.execute(\"SHOW SLAVE STATUS\")\n    \n    def start_slave(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Start replication slave.\"\"\"\n        return self.execute(\"START SLAVE\")\n    \n    def stop_slave(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Stop replication slave.\"\"\"\n        return self.execute(\"STOP SLAVE\")\n    \n    def reset_slave(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Reset replication slave.\"\"\"\n        return self.execute(\"RESET SLAVE\")\n    \n    def create_replication_user(self, username: str, password: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Create replication user.\"\"\"\n        return self.execute(f\"CREATE REPLICATION USER {username} IDENTIFIED BY {password}\")\n    \n    def close(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Close connection.\"\"\"\n        if self.socket:\n            try:\n                self._send(\"QUIT\")\n            except:\n                pass\n            finally:\n                self.socket.close()\n                self.socket = None\n                self._connected = False\n                self._authenticated = False\n    \n    def is_connected(self) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Check if connected.\"\"\"\n        return self._connected\n    \n    def is_authenticated(self) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Check if authenticated.\"\"\"\n        return self._authenticated\n    \n    def current_database(self) -> Optional[str]:\n        \"\"\"Get current database name.\"\"\"\n        return self._current_db\n    \n    # Private methods\n    \n    def _send(self, cmd: str) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Send command to server.\"\"\"\n        self.socket.sendall(f\"{cmd}\\n\".encode(self.encoding))\n    \n    def _read_line(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Read a line from socket.\"\"\"\n        data = self.socket.recv(4096)\n        if not data:\n            raise ConnectionError(\"Connection closed by server\")\n        return data.decode(self.encoding).strip()\n    \n    def _read_lines(self, count: int) -> List[str]:\n        \"\"\"Read multiple lines.\"\"\"\n        return [self._read_line() for _ in range(count)]\n    \n    def _read_response(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Read complete response.\"\"\"\n        response = []\n        start_time = __import__('time').time()\n        \n        while True:\n            # Timeout check\n            if __import__('time').time() - start_time > self.timeout:\n                raise TimeoutError(\"Read timeout\")\n            \n            line = self._read_line()\n            \n            if not line:\n                continue\n            \n            response.append(line)\n            \n            # End markers\n            if (line.startswith((\"OK:\", \"ERROR:\", \"BYE\")) or\n                \"row(s) in set\" in line or\n                line == \"Empty set\"):\n                break\n        \n        return \"\\n\".join(response)\n    \n    def _parse_select_result(self, text: str) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Parse SELECT result into list of dictionaries.\n        \n        Args:\n            text: Raw response text\n            \n        Returns:\n            List of row dictionaries\n        \"\"\"\n        lines = text.strip().split(\"\\n\")\n        rows = []\n        headers = []\n        \n        for line in lines:\n            line = line.strip()\n            \n            # Skip separators\n            if line.startswith(\"+-\"):\n                continue\n            \n            # Parse header\n            if line.startswith(\"|\") and not headers:\n                headers = [h.strip() for h in line.split(\"|\")[1:-1]]\n                continue\n            \n            # Parse data row\n            if line.startswith(\"|\") and headers:\n                values = [v.strip() for v in line.split(\"|\")[1:-1]]\n                if len(values) == len(headers):\n                    row = {}\n                    for i, header in enumerate(headers):\n                        # Try to convert to int/float\n                        val = values[i]\n                        if val == \"NULL\":\n                            row[header] = None\n                        else:\n                            try:\n                                row[header] = int(val)\n                            except ValueError:\n                                try:\n                                    row[header] = float(val)\n                                except ValueError:\n                                    row[header] = val\n                    rows.append(row)\n        \n        return rows\n    \n    def _parse_list_result(self, text: str) -> List[str]:\n        \"\"\"Parse SHOW DATABASES/TABLES result.\"\"\"\n        lines = text.strip().split(\"\\n\")\n        items = []\n        for line in lines:\n            if line.startswith(\"OK:\"):\n                continue\n            if line.strip():\n                items.append(line.strip())\n        return items\n    \n    def __enter__(self) -> 'LevelDBClient':\n        \"\"\"Context manager entry.\"\"\"\n        return self.connect()\n    \n    def __exit__(self, exc_type, exc_val, exc_tb) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Context manager exit.\"\"\"\n        self.close()\n        return False\n    \n    def __repr__(self) -> str:\n        return f\"LevelDBClient({self.host}:{self.port})\"\n\n\nclass AuthenticationError(Exception):\n    \"\"\"Authentication failed.\"\"\"\n    pass\n\n\n# Context manager for easy connection handling\n@contextmanager\ndef connect(host: str = 'localhost', port: int = 9999,\n            username: str = 'admin', password: str = 'admin'):\n    \"\"\"\n    Context manager for database connections.\n    \n    Example:\n        with connect('localhost', 9999, 'admin', 'admin') as db:\n            db.create_database('test')\n            result = db.select('users')\n    \"\"\"\n    client = LevelDBClient(host, port)\n    try:\n        client.connect()\n        client.auth(username, password)\n        yield client\n    finally:\n        client.close()\n\n\n# Async client for high-performance applications\nclass AsyncLevelDBClient:\n    \"\"\"\n    Async client for LevelDB Socket Server.\n    Requires Python 3.7+ with asyncio.\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, host: str = 'localhost', port: int = 9999):\n        self.host = host\n        self.port = port\n        self.reader = None\n        self.writer = None\n    \n    async def connect(self):\n        \"\"\"Connect to server.\"\"\"\n        self.reader, self.writer = await __import__('asyncio').open_connection(\n            self.host, self.port\n        )\n        # Read welcome\n        for _ in range(6):\n            await self.reader.readline()\n        return self\n    \n    async def auth(self, username: str, password: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Authenticate.\"\"\"\n        self.writer.write(f\"USER {username}\\n\".encode())\n        await self.writer.drain()\n        await self.reader.readline()\n        \n        self.writer.write(f\"PASS {password}\\n\".encode())\n        await self.writer.drain()\n        response = (await self.reader.readline()).decode()\n        return response.startswith(\"OK\")\n    \n    async def execute(self, sql: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Execute command.\"\"\"\n        self.writer.write(f\"{sql}\\n\".encode())\n        await self.writer.drain()\n        \n        response = []\n        while True:\n            line = (await self.reader.readline()).decode().strip()\n            response.append(line)\n            if line.startswith((\"OK:\", \"ERROR:\")):\n                break\n        return \"\\n\".join(response)\n    \n    async def close(self):\n        \"\"\"Close connection.\"\"\"\n        if self.writer:\n            self.writer.write(b\"QUIT\\n\")\n            await self.writer.drain()\n            self.writer.close()\n            await self.writer.wait_closed()\n    \n    async def __aenter__(self):\n        return await self.connect()\n    \n    async def __aexit__(self, exc_type, exc_val, exc_tb):\n        await self.close()\n        return False\n\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    # Demo usage\n    print(\"LevelDB Python Client Library\")\n    print(\"=\" * 50)\n <!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "<WriteFile><fileName>examples/python/replication_example.py</fileName><contentOfFile>#!/usr/bin/env python3\n\"\"\"\nLevelDB Python Client - Replication Example\n\nThis example demonstrates working with replication features.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport time\nfrom leveldb_client import LevelDBClient, connect\n\n\ndef main():\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n    print(\"LevelDB Python Client - Replication Example\")\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n    \n    try:\n        # Wait for replication\n        print(\"\\nWaiting 3 seconds for replication...\")\n        time.sleep(3)\n        \n        # Check data on slave\n        print(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 60)\n        print(\"Checking data on SLAVE:\")\n        print(\"=\" * 60)\n        slave.use('replication_test')\n        data = slave.select('sync_data')\n        \n        if data:\n            for row in data:\n                print(f\"  ID: {row['id']}, Message: {row['message']}, \"\n                      f\"Time: {row['timestamp']}\")\n        else:\n            print(\"  No data yet (replication might still be in progress)\")\n        \n        # close\n2. **Reuse connections** when making multiple queries\n3. **Handle exceptions** properly in production code\n4. **Use prepared statements** concept - validate inputs before sending\n5. **Set appropriate timeouts** based on your network latency\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Connection Refused\n- Check if server is running: `python server.py`\n- Verify host and port are correct\n- Check firewall settings\n\n### Authentication Failed\n- Verify username and password\n- Check if user exists: `SHOW USERS` as admin\n- Create user if needed: `CREATE REPLICATION USER`\n\n### Timeout\n-
